- `GET /api/setup/env-check` - required/optional env status, `missingRequired`, `databaseState` (`set` | `provisioned-redeploying` [checked via Vercel API] | `missing`), `neonAvailable`, `vercelConfigured`, `localMode`.
- `POST /api/setup/vercel-connect` - `list-projects` (token validation, projects + domains) | `list-account-domains` (every domain on the account/team owning the project, so already-bought domains can be attached) | `add-domain` (attaches a domain to the project; returns its full `DomainState`; a 409 from a re-add of an already-attached domain is reported as that domain's current state, not an error) | `domain-status` (re-reads a domain's `DomainState`, first POSTing Vercel's `/domains/{d}/verify` so a freshly-added ownership TXT is actually re-checked) | `configure` (writes VERCEL_API_TOKEN, VERCEL_PROJECT_ID, generated SESSION_SECRET + ENCRYPTION_KEY, SITE_URL, NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_URL, optional NEON_API_KEY, GITHUB_REPO from the project's git link; deliberately does not redeploy yet). `DomainState` = `{ name, verified, verification[], misconfigured, recommended }` - `misconfigured` (from `GET /v6/domains/{d}/config`) means DNS isn't pointing at Vercel, `!verified` (from `GET /v9/projects/{p}/domains/{d}`) means Vercel hasn't accepted the ownership TXT challenge; the two are independent and both gate the wizard's Configure button. `.vercel.app` aliases short-circuit to ready.
- `POST /api/setup/configure-env` - writes optional allowlisted env vars during the wizard.
- `POST /api/setup/provision-db` - actions: `list` (Neon projects incl. org-scoped) | `check-existing` (counts user tables) | `save-url` (user-supplied DATABASE_URL → Vercel + redeploy) | `use-existing` (pooled URI via Neon API, optional `destroyData` = DROP SCHEMA public on the direct endpoint) | `create` (default: Neon project `cactus-<vercelProjectId>`, Postgres 18, chosen region, idempotent by name search; writes DATABASE_URL + NEON_PROJECT_ID; redeploys) | `ensure-redeploy` (self-heal for the "provisioned, awaiting redeploy" state: returns the in-flight deployment if one is running, otherwise triggers a fresh one; `status: 'missing'` if DATABASE_URL isn't in the Vercel env after all). Credentials may come from the body pre-redeploy. Env writes go through `upsertVercelEnvVars` (overwrites stale values; sensitive vars skip the `development` target Vercel rejects). Provisioning responses carry `deploymentId` on success or `redeployError` when the trigger failed - the wizard shows the error with a retry instead of a phantom "Redeploying…". No short-circuit on a stale DATABASE_URL already sitting in Vercel env vars.
- `POST /api/setup/read-state` - wizard resume state; 404 once complete.
- `POST /api/setup/create-admin` - seeds core permissions, ensures the protected Admin role, creates the admin user (email verification exempt); exact-match retry path preserves the WebAuthn user handle and clears stale passkeys.
- `POST /api/setup/set-admin-path` - 3–64 chars `[a-z0-9-]`, blocklisted values rejected; upserts SiteConfig.
- `GET /api/setup/suggest-path` - random `word-suffix` admin path suggestion.
- `POST /api/setup/essentials` - siteName + timezone.
- `POST /api/setup/complete` - seeds Home page (slug `home`, published), Main Menu, the default layouts (`seedDefaultLayouts`, not "all starters" - see `lib/setup/`), the Styles draft page; sets `setupCompleted`, status `comingSoon`, `hideFromCrawlers`, default design tokens; Edge Config sync; generates missing SESSION_SECRET/ENCRYPTION_KEY (Vercel write + redeploy, returns `needsRedeploy`, plus `redeployError` if the trigger failed so the wizard can point at a manual redeploy) or auto-logs the admin in; stamps `SiteConfig.starterTemplatesVersion`. Re-POST after setup is refused 403.
- `POST /api/setup/reset` - sets `setupCompleted = false`, only when zero users exist.
- `GET /api/setup/deployment-logs` - Vercel deployment state + log lines with a `since` cursor; post-setup requires session + `config.manage` and the server's own token; pre-setup accepts the wizard's token in the **`x-vercel-token` header** (never `?token=` - a live API credential in a URL lands in access logs and browser history) plus `?projectId=` for team-scope resolution. The setup-complete check tolerates a missing database (pre-setup there is none - previously this 500'd and the wizard never showed deploy state). Passes `teamId` to the Vercel API for team-owned projects.

GitHub App connect flow (under `app/cactus-admin/integrations/github/`, reached via the admin path rewrite):

- `GET start` (`config.manage`) - builds the GitHub App manifest (name "Cactus Foundation - {siteName}", permissions `contents: write` + `metadata: read`); state cookie `cactus_github_app_state` (10 min).
- `GET callback` (session) - state check; converts the manifest code via `POST /app-manifests/{code}/conversions`; encrypts pem/webhook secret/client id/client secret with `ENCRYPTION_KEY`; replaces the GithubAppConnection row; uploads `cactus.svg` as the app logo (non-fatal); redirects with `github=connected|error&reason=…`.
- `GET install` (`config.manage`) - returns `github.com/apps/<slug>/installations/new` URL + state cookie.
- `GET installed` (session) - stores `installation_id` and the installation account login.
- `POST disconnect` (`config.manage`) - deletes the GithubAppConnection rows (the App itself remains on GitHub).

Loading/error boundaries: none exist (no `loading.tsx`, `error.tsx`, or `global-error.tsx` files in `app/`).

### Middleware

There is no `middleware.ts`. `proxy.ts` at the repo root is the Next.js 16 replacement, running on the Node runtime (so it uses Prisma directly).

- Matcher: everything except `_next/static`, `_next/image`, and static file extensions (ico/png/jpg/jpeg/svg/webp/gif/woff/woff2/ttf/eot/css/js).
- Security headers (production only; skipped in development): CSP (`default-src 'self'`; scripts `'unsafe-inline' 'unsafe-eval'`; styles allow Google Fonts; img allows self/data/blob/picsum/the Worker host; `frame-ancestors 'none'`; `form-action 'self' https://github.com`), `X-Frame-Options: DENY`, `X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff`, `Referrer-Policy: strict-origin-when-cross-origin`, Permissions-Policy (camera/mic/geolocation off, WebAuthn self), HSTS 2 years preload.
- Always-pass paths: `/api/health`, `/api/webhooks/`, `/_next/`, `/favicon.ico`.
- Direct requests to `/cactus-admin*` return 404.
- Direct requests to `/cactus-account*` return 404 (Members system internal prefix, `MEMBER_INTERNAL` from `lib/members/paths.ts`).
- First-run gate: until `setupCompleted && userCount > 0`, everything redirects to `/setup` except `/setup`, `/api/setup`, `/api/auth/passkey/`, `/api/auth/totp/`, `/api/health`, `/_next/`, `/favicon.ico`. After setup, `/setup*` returns 404.
- Admin path enforcement: resolves the admin path from Edge Config (when write creds present) else a 5-second-TTL Prisma cache; rewrites `/<adminPath>/*` → `/cactus-admin/*`. The `/login` sub-path is rewritten without an auth check (header `x-cactus-is-login: 1`). All other sub-paths validate the `cactus_session` cookie; on success sets `x-cactus-admin-path`, `x-cactus-user-id`, `x-cactus-role-protected`; unauthenticated requests redirect to `/<adminPath>/login?next=…`. (The former full-page redeploy trap is gone - in-flight redeploys are surfaced by the admin shell's `DeployStatusBar` and the notification bell instead.)
- Member-area path rewrite: unconditionally rewrites `/<memberAreaPath>/*` → `/cactus-account/*` (sets `x-cactus-member-path` and `x-cactus-member-full-path` - the latter is the original public pathname+search, used by `app/(public)/cactus-account/layout.tsx` to build an accurate post-login `?redirect=` since the internal pathname alone can't reconstruct it), checked after admin enforcement so admin wins any prefix collision. Still no session validation in proxy itself - the account layout does its own gate. Unlike the admin rewrite, this currently runs before the site-status gate below, so member pages stay reachable during comingSoon/maintenance; revisit when Phase 8 wires `siteWideMembersOnly`.
- API requests pass through, with a CSRF origin check on non-GET/HEAD/OPTIONS: a present-but-mismatched `Origin` header returns 403.
- `/page-preview/` and `/layout-preview/` always pass (so editors can preview while the site is gated).
- Site status gate: when status ≠ `live`, public routes are rewritten to `/cactus-status/coming-soon` or `/cactus-status/maintenance` unless the session's role `isProtected`.
- Members-only site access (Phase 8 of MEMBERS_SPEC.md, runs after the status gate, only for ordinary public content - admin/api/preview/member-area paths have already returned by this point): gated when `membersConfig.siteWideMembersOnly` is on OR the path resolves to a non-`PUBLIC` module route tier (`lib/members/access.ts`'s `resolveRouteTier`, cached module read). `siteWideMembersOnlyExceptions` prefix-exempts a path outright; admins bypass; else the `cactus_member_session` cookie is validated (`TRUSTED_MEMBER` tiers additionally require `member.trusted`). Unsatisfied + `guestPreviewEnabled` → passes through with `x-cactus-guest-preview: 1` (consumed by the Puck `MemberGate`/`TrustedMemberGate` blocks' teaser rendering only, for now). Unsatisfied + no preview: no session → redirect to `/{memberAreaPath}/login?redirect=…`; signed in but insufficient tier → 404 (no sensible redirect target, no dedicated status page for this case).

### Environment Variables

Core:

- `DATABASE_URL` - PostgreSQL pooled connection string. Required. Consumed by Prisma (`lib/db/prisma.ts`), build scripts, setup routes.
- `DIRECT_URL` - optional non-pooled connection for migrations; `scripts/build-migrate.mjs` (falls back to stripping `-pooler` from DATABASE_URL).
- `SESSION_SECRET` - HMAC ingredient for session/trusted-device token hashing, min 32 chars. Required (auto-generated on Vercel during setup). `lib/config/env.ts:getSessionSecret`, `lib/auth/session.ts`.
- `SITE_URL` - canonical public URL; also the WebAuthn rpId/origin source. Required. `lib/config/env.ts` (`getSiteUrl`, `getWebAuthnRpId`, `getWebAuthnOrigin`), robots/sitemap, recovery links.
- `NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_URL` - browser-visible copy of SITE_URL shown in the setup wizard. Optional in code, written by setup.
- `VERCEL` - platform-injected. Its absence defines local-development mode (`isLocalMode()` in `lib/config/env.ts`), which disables env editing, redeploys, and core/module updates.
- `VERCEL_URL` - platform-injected fallback for site URL in robots/sitemap.
- `NODE_ENV` - dev/prod switches (security headers, cookie `secure`, WebAuthn localhost overrides, Prisma logging).
- `NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_VERSION` - injected by `next.config.ts` from `package.json` version.
- `NEXT_TELEMETRY_DISABLED` - set to `1` by `next.config.ts`.
- `PORT` - `scripts/dev-warm.sh` only (default 3000).

Vercel control plane:

- `VERCEL_API_TOKEN` - required on Vercel; env-var writes, redeploys, deployment logs/status, Edge Config writes. `lib/vercel/env.ts`, `lib/vercel/deploy.ts`, `lib/deploy/redeploy.ts`, setup + admin env routes.
- `VERCEL_PROJECT_ID` - required on Vercel; identifies the project for all of the above.
- `EDGE_CONFIG` - optional; Edge Config read connection string (`lib/config/edge-config.ts`, `@vercel/edge-config`).
- `VERCEL_EDGE_CONFIG_ID` - optional; Edge Config item writes via the Vercel REST API.
- `VERCEL_WEBHOOK_SECRET` - optional; verifies `/api/webhooks/vercel` (Pro/Enterprise; Hobby falls back to lazy polling).

Auth:

- `TURNSTILE_SITE_KEY` / `TURNSTILE_SECRET_KEY` - optional; Cloudflare Turnstile on login/register/recovery and module forms. `lib/auth/turnstile.ts` fails open when unset, fails closed on network errors when set.
- `MEMBER_AREA_PATH` - optional; public URL prefix for the member account area (default `account`). Deploy-time only, changing it requires a redeploy. Read via `getMemberAreaPath()` in `lib/members/paths.ts` (sanitised, blocklist-checked, falls back to the default). Member-area pages live internally at `/cactus-account/*`, rewritten in `proxy.ts` (see Middleware section).

GitHub:

- `GITHUB_API_TOKEN` - optional; PAT fallback for all GitHub operations (`lib/github/client.ts`), `scripts/sync-wiki.mjs`.
- `GITHUB_REPO` - `owner/repo` of the site's own repository; module registry commits and core-update pushes (`lib/modules/github.ts`, `lib/updates/core.ts`).
- `CACTUS_CORE_REPO` - optional upstream override for core updates; defaults to `usersaynoso/cactus-foundation` (`lib/updates/core.ts`).
- `WIKI_SOURCE_REPO` - optional; `scripts/sync-wiki.mjs` (defaults to GITHUB_REPO).

Encryption:

- `ENCRYPTION_KEY` - 64-char hex (32 bytes) AES-256-GCM key. Required for the GitHub App flow, TOTP secret storage, and the reply-catcher module's mailbox credentials. `lib/crypto/secrets.ts`.

Neon:

- `NEON_API_KEY` - optional; automatic database provisioning during setup (`/api/setup/provision-db`).
- `NEON_PROJECT_ID` - written by provisioning; surfaced by `/api/auth/config` for the lost-passkey Neon console deep link.

Media (one provider active at a time; per-provider keys defined in `lib/media/providers.ts`):

- `B2_APPLICATION_KEY_ID`, `B2_APPLICATION_KEY`, `B2_BUCKET_NAME`, `B2_ENDPOINT` - Backblaze B2.
- `R2_ACCOUNT_ID`, `R2_ACCESS_KEY_ID`, `R2_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY`, `R2_BUCKET_NAME` - Cloudflare R2.
- `S3_ACCESS_KEY_ID`, `S3_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY`, `S3_BUCKET_NAME`, `S3_REGION` - AWS S3.
- `SPACES_ACCESS_KEY_ID`, `SPACES_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY`, `SPACES_BUCKET_NAME`, `SPACES_REGION` - DigitalOcean Spaces.
- `WASABI_ACCESS_KEY_ID`, `WASABI_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY`, `WASABI_BUCKET_NAME`, `WASABI_REGION` - Wasabi.
- `MINIO_ENDPOINT`, `MINIO_ACCESS_KEY_ID`, `MINIO_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY`, `MINIO_BUCKET_NAME`, `MINIO_USE_SSL` - MinIO.
- `BLOB_READ_WRITE_TOKEN` - Vercel Blob.
- `SUPABASE_STORAGE_PROJECT_URL`, `SUPABASE_STORAGE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY`, `SUPABASE_STORAGE_BUCKET_NAME` - Supabase Storage.
- `CLOUDINARY_CLOUD_NAME`, `CLOUDINARY_API_KEY`, `CLOUDINARY_API_SECRET` - Cloudinary (direct).
- `IMAGEKIT_PUBLIC_KEY`, `IMAGEKIT_PRIVATE_KEY`, `IMAGEKIT_URL_ENDPOINT` - ImageKit (direct).
- `CLOUDFLARE_WORKER_URL` - shared Worker URL for all proxied providers; required by every proxied provider (`envKeysForProvider` appends it).
- `CLOUDFLARE_WORKER_HOSTNAME` - Worker hostname for `next.config.ts` remotePatterns and the proxy CSP img-src. Optional: when unset, both derive it from `CLOUDFLARE_WORKER_URL` (`workerImageHost()` in `proxy.ts` and `next.config.ts`), so the admin auto-deploy needs no extra env var.
- `NEXT_PUBLIC_CLOUDFLARE_WORKER_URL` - client-side Worker URL fallback used by the custom image loader (`lib/media/loader.ts`).

Email:

- `BREVO_API_KEY` - Brevo transactional API; takes priority over SMTP. `lib/email/index.ts`.
- `SMTP_HOST`, `SMTP_PORT` (default 587), `SMTP_USER`, `SMTP_PASS` - nodemailer SMTP fallback.

Other:

- `SENTRY_DSN` - optional. Read only for configured-status display (dashboard, env editor); no Sentry SDK is installed or initialised anywhere.
- `CRON_SECRET` - reply-catcher module; Vercel attaches it as `Authorization: Bearer` on cron invocations of `/api/m/contact-form-reply-catcher/cron/poll`.
- `PRISMA_SCHEMA_DISABLE_ADVISORY_LOCK` - set to `1` by `scripts/build-migrate.mjs` at build time only.

Cloudflare Worker (separate deployment, `workers/media-worker`): `ALLOWED_ORIGIN`, `BLOB_BASE_URL`, plus the same provider secret sets as above, configured via `wrangler secret put`.

### Database Schema

Single Prisma schema at `prisma/schema.prisma` (PostgreSQL). One init migration: `prisma/migrations/20260626000000_init/migration.sql`. All timestamps UTC.

- `User` - `id` (cuid PK), `email` (unique), `username` (unique), `displayName?`, `passwordHash?`, `roleId` → Role, `emailVerifiedAt?`, `createdAt`, `updatedAt`, `suspendedAt?`, `acceptedPrivacyPolicyAt?`, `totpSecretEncrypted?`, `totpVerifiedAt?`, `totpLastStep? BigInt`, `smsOtpPhoneEncrypted?` (AES-256-GCM phone; when set and an SMS provider module is active, password-login OTPs go by text). Relations: passkeys, sessions, trustedDevices, emailChallenges, recoveryRequests, infoPages, mediaItems, consentRecords. Indexes: email, username.
- `Passkey` - `id`, `userId` → User (cascade), `credentialId` (unique), `publicKey Bytes`, `counter BigInt default 0`, `transports String[]`, `label?`, `createdAt`. Index: userId.
- `Session` - `id`, `userId` → User (cascade), `tokenHash` (unique; sha256(token + SESSION_SECRET)), `createdAt`, `expiresAt`. Indexes: userId, expiresAt.
- `TrustedDevice` - `id`, `userId` → User (cascade), `tokenHash` (unique), `createdAt`, `expiresAt`. Indexes: userId, expiresAt.
- `EmailChallenge` - `id`, `userId` → User (cascade), `codeHash`, `purpose` (`login_otp` | `verify_email` | `recovery`), `expiresAt`, `attempts Int default 0`, `createdAt`. Indexes: (userId, purpose), expiresAt.
- `RecoveryRequest` - `id`, `userId` → User (cascade), `tokenHash` (unique), `createdAt`, `expiresAt`, `used Boolean default false`. Indexes: userId, expiresAt.
- `Role` - `id`, `name` (unique), `isProtected Boolean default false`, `createdAt`. Relations: users, members, permissions. A protected `"Members"` row is lazily created (name-unique-race-safe) the first time anyone registers via `/api/members/register` (`lib/members/default-role.ts`), and assigned as every new Member's `roleId`.
- `Permission` - `key` (PK), `description?`, `module?` (null = core, else the registering module name). Relation: rolePermissions.
- `RolePermission` - composite PK (roleId, permissionKey); both FKs cascade.
- `SiteConfig` - singleton (`id = "singleton"`): `siteName` (default "My Cactus Site"), `tagline?`, `description?`, `timezone` ("UTC"), `locale` ("en-GB"), `dateFormat` ("DD/MM/YYYY"), `timeFormat` ("HH:mm"), `adminPath` (unique), `setupCompleted` (false), `status SiteStatus` (comingSoon), `hideFromCrawlers` (true), `trustDeviceDays` (28), `starterTemplatesVersion?` (core version whose starter templates were last seeded; mismatch with `package.json` version triggers `ensureStarterLayoutsCurrent`'s auto-refresh), `emailFromName?`, `emailFromAddress?`, `emailProvider?` ('brevo' | 'smtp'), `mediaProvider MediaProviderType?`, `privacyPolicyPageId?`, `termsPageId?`, `logoMediaId?`, `logoDarkMediaId?` (optional dark-mode logo; frontend swaps to it via CSS keyed on `data-theme="dark"`), `faviconMediaId?`, `faviconDarkMediaId?` (optional dark-mode favicon; served via a `prefers-color-scheme: dark` media query, so it follows the browser/OS scheme not the in-site toggle), `appIconMediaId?` (square source image the admin uploads; favicon/apple/PWA icons auto-generated from it), `appleTouchIconMediaId?`, `webManifest192MediaId?`, `webManifest512MediaId?` (each independently overridable), `appName?`, `appShortName?`, `themeColor?`, `backgroundColor?` (web-app manifest identity; fall back to `siteName`/white via `lib/config/branding.ts`), `sessionPurgeAfterDays` (30), `recoveryPurgeAfterDays` (7), `mainMenuId?`, `homepageId?`, `pendingRedeployId?`, `pendingRedeployAt?`, `designTokens Json?`, `consentBannerConfig Json?`, `coreUpdateChannel` ("public"), `membersConfig Json?` (Members settings, Zod-parsed with defaults by `lib/members/config.ts`), `createdAt`, `updatedAt`.
- `UserColourPreset` - user-created Styles > Colours presets: `id`, `name` (unique), `tokens Json` (`{primary:{light,dark}, linkColour, linkHoverColour, linkColourDark, linkHoverColourDark}` - same shape as the hardcoded `ColourPreset` in `lib/design/tokens.ts`), `createdAt`, `updatedAt`. The 10 default presets (`COLOUR_PRESETS`) are still hardcoded in app code with no DB row and can't be overwritten/deleted through this model; the Styles preset bar shows these user rows first, then the defaults.
- `InfoPage` - `id`, `slug` (unique), `title`, `body Text`, `bodyFormat BodyFormat` (markdown), `builderData Json?` (working draft; autosave target), `publishedData Json?` (live content, written only by Publish), `publishedAt?`, `publishedById?` (no relation), `history Json?` (array of `{data, title, at, byId}`, max 10, newest first), `status PageStatus` (draft), `metaDescription?`, `ogImageId?` (Media id, no relation), `createdById?` → User (SetNull), `createdAt`, `updatedAt`. Relation: menuItems. Indexes: slug, status.
- `Media` - `id`, `key` (unique), `provider MediaProviderType`, `url`, `uploadedById?` → User (SetNull), `altText?`, `isDecorative` (false), `originalName?` (the filename the user uploaded, kept verbatim for display since `key` is deliberately mangled with a nanoid prefix; null for legacy rows + generated files - icons/avatars/exports - which fall back to the key basename; the media library card/lightbox/grid and the Puck media picker all show `originalName || key.split('/').pop()`, and both the `/api/admin/media` GET and the media library page search it alongside key/altText), `mimeType`, `sizeBytes Int`, `optimised` (Boolean, false - set true once the media library's in-place optimise has re-encoded the item to WebP, drives the "Optimised" badge and stops it being offered again), `folderId?` → Folder (SetNull; null = library root; the folder's path is baked into the item's `key`/`url`), `tags MediaTag[]`, `createdAt`. Indexes: uploadedById, createdAt, provider, folderId.
- `Folder` - media library folder. `id`, `name`, `parentId?` → Folder self-relation "FolderTree" (`onDelete:Cascade`; null = root), `children Folder[]`, `media Media[]`, `createdAt`. `@@unique([parentId, name])` (root uniqueness also enforced in app since Postgres treats null parentId rows as distinct), index parentId. Folders are physical: the sanitised slash-joined ancestor path lives in each contained item's storage key/url, so rename/move/delete relocate or remove blobs (see `lib/media/organise.ts`).
- `Tag` - `id`, `name` (unique), `createdAt`, `media MediaTag[]`. Freeform, created on the fly.
- `MediaTag` - join: `mediaId` + `tagId` (composite PK), both FKs `onDelete:Cascade`, index tagId.
- `MediaMigrationJob` - `id`, `toProvider MediaProviderType`, `status` (pending | running | completed | failed | cancelled), `totalItems Int`, `migratedItems Int default 0`, `failedItemIds Json default []`, `cursor?`, `startedAt`, `completedAt?`, `lastError?`. Indexes: status, startedAt.
- `Layout` - `id`, `name`, `type` (header | footer | infoPage | notFound | statusPage | module type; default infoPage), `description?`, `builderData Json?` (working draft; autosave target), `publishedData Json?` (live content, written only on publish), `publishedAt?`, `publishedById?` (no relation), `history Json?` (array of `{data, title, at, byId}`, max 10, newest first - mirrors InfoPage), `displayConditions Json?` (`{include: Rule[], exclude: Rule[]}`), `priority Int default 0`, `status PageStatus` (draft), `createdAt`, `updatedAt`. (`isStarter Boolean` is **gone** - starter templates are in-code data now. `prisma/core-reconcile/005_retire_starter_layouts.sql` deletes the legacy starter rows and then drops the column and its index; the init migration no longer creates either, and `004_perf_indexes.sql` no longer indexes it - leaving that `CREATE INDEX` in place would have failed every build after the column was dropped.)
- `SavedBlock` - reusable Puck block snapshots, shared by the page and layout builders: `id`, `name`, `componentType` (the Puck component type, e.g. "Hero"), `data Json` (full ComponentData blob, reinserted verbatim on use), `createdAt`. Single-tenant, no categories/folders.
- `Module` - `id`, `name` (unique), `repoUrl`, `version` (confirmed live tag), `pendingVersion?` (in-flight target, promoted only on deploy success), `tablePrefix` (unique), `status ModuleStatus` (pending_install), `installedAt`, `lastError?`, `lastCheckedAt?`, `updateAvailable?`, `updateNotes? Text`, `updateChannel` ("public"), `manifest Json?` (parsed cactus.module.json), `layoutsSeededAt?` (set the one time this module's `publishByDefault` layouts were stamped, by `markModulesDeploySucceeded()`; never cleared, because a module *update* redeploys down the same path and a create-only upsert would resurrect layouts the owner deleted).
- `Notification` - `id`, `type NotificationType` (deployment), `title`, `reasons Json?` (deployment type: `{label, detail?, at}[]`), `link?` (admin-relative), `dedupeKey?` (core-update, module-update:{id}, contact-form:messages), `readAt?` (null = unread, drives nav badge), `deployInitiatedAt?` (null = open deployment notification), `createdAt`, `updatedAt`. Indexes: (type, deployInitiatedAt), readAt, dedupeKey.
- `ModuleMigration` - `id`, `moduleName`, `migrationName`, `appliedAt`, `checksum` (sha256 of the SQL). Unique (moduleName, migrationName); index moduleName. Tracked separately from Prisma's own history.
- `DeployLock` - singleton: `id = "singleton"`, `lockedAt`, `lockedBy` (module or update identifier). Prevents concurrent installs/updates.
- `GithubAppConnection` - `id`, `appId`, `appSlug`, `installationId?`, `installationAccount?`, `privateKeyEncrypted Text`, `webhookSecretEncrypted? Text`, `clientIdEncrypted? Text`, `clientSecretEncrypted? Text`, `createdAt`, `updatedAt`. Secrets AES-256-GCM encrypted with ENCRYPTION_KEY.
- `Menu` - `id`, `name`, `createdAt`, `updatedAt`. Relation: items.
- `MenuItem` - `id`, `menuId` → Menu (cascade), `parentId?` self-relation (cascade), `type MenuItemType`, `pageId?` → InfoPage (cascade), `label?`, `url?`, `moduleId?`, `entityKind?`, `entityId?` (MODULE_ENTITY target - no FK, module tables live outside Prisma, resolved via `core.menu-entity-provider`), `openInNewTab` (false), `order Int`, `createdAt`, `updatedAt`. Unique (menuId, pageId); indexes menuId, pageId.
- `RateLimit` - `id`, `key` (`ip:<addr>` | `account:<id>` | `account_email:<email>` | `consent:<id>`), `action`, `attempts Int default 1`, `windowStart`. Unique (key, action); index windowStart. In-database rate limiting with atomic INSERT … ON CONFLICT.
- `ConsentRecord` - append-only: `id`, `consentId`, `userId?` → User (SetNull), `categoriesVersion Int`, `decision Json`, `action` (accept_all | reject_all | custom | withdraw | acknowledge), `ipTruncated?`, `uaHash?`, `createdAt`. Indexes (consentId, createdAt), userId.
- `WebAuthnChallenge` - transient: `id`, `userId?`, `memberId?` (member passkey flows), `challenge` (unique), `purpose` (registration | authentication | member_registration | member_authentication), `expiresAt` (5 min), `createdAt`. Indexes userId, memberId, expiresAt.

Members system (all cuid PKs, all token/code columns store hashes only, every child table FKs `Member` with cascade delete; see MEMBERS_SPEC.md):

- `Member` - `id`, `email` (unique), `username` (unique, stored lowercase), `displayName?`, `avatarMediaId?` (Media id, no relation), `avatarChoice AvatarChoice` (GENERATED), `bio?`, `websiteUrl?`, `trusted` (false), `status MemberStatus` (PENDING_VERIFICATION), `roleId?` → Role (SetNull; assigned to the seeded "Members" role at registration, nullable for rows predating the field), `emailVerified` (false), `emailVerifiedAt?`, `backupEmail?`, `suspendedUntil?`, `suspensionReason?`, `suspensionNotified` (false), `deletionRequestedAt?`, `deletionScheduledAt?`, `deletionExportReady` (false), `usernameChangedAt?`, `previousUsername?`, `previousUsernameExpiresAt?`, `createdAt`, `updatedAt`. Indexes: status, previousUsername, deletionScheduledAt, createdAt.
- `MemberPasskey` - `credentialId` (unique), `publicKey Bytes`, `counter BigInt default 0`, `transports String[]`, `deviceName?`, `lastUsedAt?`. Index memberId.
- `MemberPassword` - one per member (`memberId` unique), bcrypt `hash`.
- `MemberTwoFactor` - `method TwoFactorMethod`, `secretEncrypted?` (AES-256-GCM TOTP secret; null for EMAIL/SMS), `phoneEncrypted?` (AES-256-GCM phone; SMS method only), `verified` (false), `lastStep? BigInt` (TOTP replay guard). Unique (memberId, method).
- `MemberTrustedBrowser` - `tokenHash` (unique), `deviceInfo?`, `expiresAt`. Indexes memberId, expiresAt.
- `MemberSession` - `tokenHash` (unique), `ipAddress?`, `userAgent?`, `location?`, `lastActiveAt`, `expiresAt`. Indexes memberId, expiresAt.
- `MemberMagicLink` / `MemberVerificationToken` - `tokenHash` (unique), `usedAt?`, `expiresAt`. Indexes memberId, expiresAt.
- `MemberEmailChallenge` - `codeHash`, `purpose` (login_2fa | setup_2fa), `expiresAt`, `attempts` (0). Indexes (memberId, purpose), expiresAt.
- `MemberRecoveryCode` - `codeHash` (unique), `usedAt?`. Index memberId.
- `MemberNotificationPreference` - `channel NotificationChannel` (EMAIL), `category` (core or module key), `digestMode DigestMode` (INSTANT), `enabled` (true). Unique (memberId, channel, category).
- `MemberConsentRecord` - `consentType`, `granted`, `ipAddress?`, `userAgent?`. Indexes memberId, createdAt.
- `MemberDataExportRequest` - `status DataExportStatus` (PENDING), `mediaId?` (Media id, no relation), `expiresAt?` (48h download cut-off), `completedAt?`. Indexes memberId, status.
- `MemberActivityEvent` - `type` (core or module key), `source?` (null = core, else module name), `metadata Json?`. Index (memberId, createdAt desc).
- `MemberProfileVisibility` - `memberId` unique; `showBio`/`showJoinDate`/`showWebsite` (all true).
- `MemberInvite` - `tokenHash` (unique), `createdById?`/`createdByName?` (admin snapshot, no relation), `usedAt?`, `usedByMemberId?`, `revokedAt?`, `expiresAt`. Index expiresAt. Single-use registration invites for INVITE_ONLY mode.
- `MemberAdminNote` - append-only: `authorId?`/`authorName?` (admin snapshot), `body Text`. Index (memberId, createdAt desc).
- `MemberAdminActionLog` - `actorId?`/`actorName?`, `action`, `detail Json?`. Index (memberId, createdAt desc).
- `EmailTemplate` - `key` (unique, e.g. `member.verify-email`), `subject`, `bodyHtml Text`, `updatedById?`. Admin overrides for code-registry defaults; absent row = default, reset deletes the row.

Enums: `SiteStatus` (live, comingSoon, maintenance); `PageStatus` (draft, published); `BodyFormat` (markdown, builder); `MediaProviderType` (B2, R2, S3, SPACES, WASABI, MINIO, VERCEL_BLOB, SUPABASE_STORAGE, CLOUDINARY, IMAGEKIT); `ModuleStatus` (pending_install, deploying, pending_deploy, active, inactive, failed, update_available); `NotificationType` (deployment, core_update, module_update, message); `MenuItemType` (PAGE, EXTERNAL, MODULE_ENTITY); `MemberStatus` (PENDING_VERIFICATION, PENDING_APPROVAL, ACTIVE, SUSPENDED, DELETED); `AvatarChoice` (UPLOAD, GRAVATAR, GENERATED); `TwoFactorMethod` (EMAIL, AUTHENTICATOR_APP, SMS); `NotificationChannel` (EMAIL); `DigestMode` (INSTANT, DAILY, WEEKLY, DISABLED); `DataExportStatus` (PENDING, PROCESSING, READY, EXPIRED).

### Authentication

WebAuthn (passkeys):

- `@simplewebauthn/server` v13 in `lib/auth/passkey.ts`; browser side `@simplewebauthn/browser` loaded on demand.
- rpName "Cactus Foundation"; rpId = hostname of SITE_URL (hard-coded `localhost` in development); origin = SITE_URL. rpId cannot change once passkeys exist.
- Challenges persisted in `WebAuthnChallenge` with a 5-minute TTL, deleted on use or expiry; verify calls extract the challenge from the assertion's `clientDataJSON`.
- Registration uses a stable user handle (userId bytes) so Safari/iCloud Keychain retries do not conflict; `excludeCredentials` from existing passkeys; `residentKey: preferred`, `userVerification: required`, `requireUserVerification: true` (both registration and authentication). Member passkeys (`lib/members/passkey.ts`) now match this exactly.
- Passkeys store credentialId, COSE public key bytes, signature counter (updated on every authentication), transports, and a label derived from the user agent ("Chrome on macOS").
- Zero-passkey accounts have **no** register-and-login path (`register-login` was deleted): a fresh attestation proves someone holds *an* authenticator, not that they hold *the account*. They sign in by password + OTP, authenticator app, or recovery link, then enrol a passkey from Account → Security.
- `authenticate-options` (admin `/api/auth/passkey/authenticate-options` + member equivalent) always returns an unscoped challenge with empty `allowCredentials` (discoverable-credential flow), byte-identical regardless of whether the email maps to an account or has a passkey - so it can't be used to enumerate registered emails or harvest stored credential IDs.
- **Step-up on enrolment:** adding a new authenticator (passkey `register-options`+`register-verify`, TOTP/2FA `setup-options`, admin + member) requires the current session to have authenticated within `STEP_UP_MAX_AGE_MS` (10 min; `isCurrentSessionFresh` / `isCurrentMemberSessionFresh`, keyed on the session row's `createdAt`). A stale session gets a 403 with `reauthRequired: true`; the first-run setup window is exempt. Prevents a borrowed unlocked browser from planting a durable sign-in method.

Sessions:

- Cookie `cactus_session`: httpOnly, SameSite=Lax, secure in production, 24-hour lifetime (`SESSION_DURATION_MS` in `lib/auth/session.ts`).
- Server stores only `sha256(token + SESSION_SECRET)` in `Session.tokenHash`. Validation (`validateSession`): row lookup by hash, expiry check (expired rows deleted on touch), suspended-user check; returns the user with role included.
- Server-side validation happens twice per admin request: in `proxy.ts` and again in the admin layout/route handlers via `getSessionFromCookie()`.
- Trusted devices: cookie `cactus_trusted`, same hashing scheme, N days from `SiteConfig.trustDeviceDays` (default 28), expiry refreshed on valid use; lets password logins skip the email OTP.

Other mechanisms:

- Password login: bcrypt (12 rounds), minimum 8 chars, Pwned Passwords k-anonymity breach check (fails open); always second-factored by a 6-digit OTP (`EmailChallenge`, 10-minute TTL, 5 attempts, sha256-hashed, timing-safe compare) unless the device is trusted. Unavailable when email is not configured. The OTP goes by SMS instead of email when `User.smsOtpPhoneEncrypted` is set and an active module contributes a configured SMS provider (`lib/auth/sms.ts` `getActiveSmsProvider()` over the generated `lib/modules/sms-providers.ts`); any SMS failure falls back silently to email, verification unchanged (`/api/auth/email-code`). Login response gained `channel`/`destination` (masked phone) for the OTP-step copy.
- TOTP: otpauth SHA1/6-digit/30s, issuer "Cactus Foundation", secret AES-256-GCM encrypted at rest, ±1 window, replay-protected via monotonically increasing `totpLastStep`.
- Recovery: 32-byte token, sha256-hashed, 30-minute TTL, single-use; completion revokes all sessions and trusted devices. The emailed link's GET hands the token to the login page via a short-lived HttpOnly `cactus_recovery_token` cookie + `?recovery=1` flag (never `?recovery_token=` in the URL, which would leak into history/logs/Referer); the POST reads it from that cookie (body token still accepted for older links) and clears it on success.
- Password change (`/api/account/password`, `/api/members/password`): on any successful change, unconditionally revokes every other session and every trusted device/browser, keeping only the caller's session. The old opt-in `signOutOtherSessions` flag is ignored (still parsed for client compatibility). Stops a pre-existing trusted device from surviving the change and bypassing OTP/2FA.
- Rate limiting: in-database (`RateLimit` table), atomic check-and-record. Admin OTP verify (`/api/auth/email-code`) keys on both `ip:` and `account:${userId}` (was IP-only). Limits: login 10/15min, register 5/60min, recovery_request 3/60min, email_code 5/15min, passkey_authenticate 20/15min, consent 30/15min, totp_verify 5/15min, member_register 5/60min, member_magic_link 5/15min, member_login 10/15min, member_2fa 5/15min (Members system).
- Turnstile: applied to login, register, and recovery-request; fail-open when unconfigured, fail-closed on network error when configured.
- CSRF: SameSite=Lax cookie plus an explicit Origin-mismatch 403 for unsafe methods in `proxy.ts`.

Admin path obfuscation:

- The real admin URL prefix is a per-site secret string (`SiteConfig.adminPath`, unique, suggested as e.g. `lemon-x7k2p9`), resolved at the proxy from Edge Config or DB and rewritten to the internal `/cactus-admin/*` tree. Direct `/cactus-admin` access 404s; wrong prefixes fall through to a plain Next.js 404 indistinguishable from any missing route.
- What it hides: the location of the login page and admin UI from casual scanning.
- What it does not protect: it is not an authentication factor. All admin API routes under `/api/admin/*` sit at fixed, guessable URLs and rely entirely on session + permission checks; the admin path leaks to anyone with a valid session.

Members authentication (Phase 2 of MEMBERS_SPEC.md, protected/isolated-diff-per-sub-feature; fully separate from everything above - no shared tables, cookies, or code):

- Cookie `cactus_member_session`: httpOnly, SameSite=Lax, secure in production, sliding expiry off `membersConfig.sessionDays` (default 30d, refreshed on every valid check). Server stores `sha256(token + SESSION_SECRET)` in `MemberSession.tokenHash` (`lib/members/session.ts`), same hashing scheme as admin sessions.
- `validateMemberSession` only returns a member whose `status` is `ACTIVE` - PENDING_VERIFICATION/PENDING_APPROVAL/SUSPENDED/DELETED are all rejected even with an unexpired session row.
- Trusted browser: cookie `cactus_member_trusted`, same scheme, `membersConfig.trustedBrowserDays` (default 30d).
- Passkeys (`lib/members/passkey.ts`, `@simplewebauthn`, same rpId/origin as admin): login with an existing passkey (`/api/members/auth/passkey/authenticate-options`+`authenticate-verify`) and adding a passkey from an authenticated session (`register-options`+`register-verify`). No bootstrap-without-a-session path - see the Routes section note on why that would be unsafe for members specifically (no narrow one-time setup window the way admin has).
- Magic link (`lib/members/magic-link.ts`): 15-minute single-use emailed link, `/api/members/auth/magic-link/request`+`consume`. This is how a brand-new member gets their *first* session (they have no passkey yet and passwords are off by default) - hence it, not passkey, is what makes `/{memberAreaPath}/login` actually usable end-to-end.
- `loginRejectionForStatus` (`lib/members/registration.ts`) is the shared status gate every login method calls before creating a session: only ACTIVE passes; PENDING_VERIFICATION returns a `redirectToVerify` hint back to the Phase 1 holding page.
- Password + mandatory 2FA (`/api/members/auth/password/login` + `2fa/verify`): only reachable when `passwordsEnabled`; a password without a `MemberTwoFactor` row is treated as unusable (403) rather than allowing a password-only session, since 2FA is mandatory whenever passwords are on - actually setting up that first 2FA method is a Phase 3 Security-page action. Trusted browser (`isMemberBrowserTrusted`) skips the 2FA step entirely. A verified `SMS` method (phone in `MemberTwoFactor.phoneEncrypted`) takes priority over other methods when an active SMS provider module can deliver; SMS codes share the member email-challenge store (`login_2fa`), so `2fa/verify` treats EMAIL and SMS identically, and delivery falls back silently to email when the provider is unavailable. Factor selection (both `password/login` and `2fa/verify`) only ever picks a `verified` factor - an unverified row (secret generated but never confirmed) never gates login, and there is no unverified fallback. Recovery codes (`lib/members/recovery-codes.ts`) are an alternate second factor for a member who's lost their email/authenticator access.
- `/{memberAreaPath}/login` (`app/(public)/cactus-account/login/page.tsx` + `components/members/LoginForm.tsx`): email + passkey attempt (falls back to a "no passkey, use a link instead" message), "email me a sign-in link", and (when `passwordsEnabled`) a password step branching into 2FA/recovery-code; auto-consumes a `?magic_token=` on load; `?redirect=` is sanitised to same-origin relative paths only (open-redirect guard) - nothing sets this param yet, it's there for Phase 3's account-layout session gate to use.
- Logout: `POST /api/members/auth/logout` (single, redirects `/logged-out`) and `POST /api/members/auth/logout-all` (every session, forces full re-auth - unlike admin's "revoke all" which preserves the caller's own).
- **Phase 2 (Authentication) is now fully built.** Phase 3 (member account area) is also complete - see the Member account API and member-area Pages entries above. Next up: Phase 4 (public profile).

### Permissions System

Core keys (registered by `seedCorePermissions()` in `lib/permissions/check.ts` at setup):

- `pages.read` - view info pages including drafts (admin page list, page GET/history APIs, page-preview route).
- `pages.write` - create/edit pages (POST/PATCH/autosave).
- `pages.publish` - publish pages (publish endpoint; also required to create a page already published).
- `pages.delete` - delete pages (single + bulk).
- `users.manage` - view and manage users (users page + API).
- `media.upload` - upload media.
- `media.delete` - delete media.
- `roles.manage` - Settings → Users → Roles subtab + role/permission APIs.
- `modules.manage` - module list/install/update/uninstall/directory; also grants GitHub App status read.
- `config.manage` - settings GET/PATCH, notifications, updates, media migration, redeploy dismiss, deployment logs, GitHub App flow.
- `menus.manage` - all menu APIs; also gates menu assignment from the page editor.
- `appearance.manage` - design-token PATCH.
- `layouts.manage` - layout read/create/update/delete/publish, and `/layout-preview/[id]`. Every layout route gates on it, reads included.
- `members.manage` / `members.list` / `members.view` / `members.edit` / `members.suspend` / `members.delete` / `members.invite` / `members.approve` / `members.trust` / `members.notes` / `members.settings` / `members.gdpr` / `members.email-templates` - Members system admin permissions (registered in Phase 0; enforcing routes/UI land in later Members phases - see MEMBERS_SPEC.md).

Module-registered keys (declared in each module's `cactus.module.json`, registered on install): `contact.view`, `contact.reply`, `contact.delete`, `contact.export` (contact-form); `replycatcher.manage` (contact-form-reply-catcher); `boards.access`, `boards.manage`, `boards.moderate` (boards); `directory.access`, `directory.manage` (directory); `gazette.access`, `gazette.contributor`, `gazette.author`, `gazette.editor` (gazette); `shop.access`, `shop.manage`, `shop.products`, `shop.orders`, `shop.customers`, `shop.discounts`, `shop.reports` (shop); `twilio.manage` (twilio). Stored in `Permission` with `module` set; deleted on module uninstall.

Where checks occur:

- Protected roles (`Role.isProtected`, only "Admin" is seeded) bypass every check (`hasPermission` short-circuits; `isAdmin()` = `role.isProtected`).
- `proxy.ts`: session validity only (plus `isProtected` for the site-status bypass and the redeploy trap); no per-permission checks.
- API routes: `getSessionFromCookie()` + `hasPermission(user, key)` per handler (see the Routes section for each route's key).
- UI: server components branch on `hasPermission`/`isAdmin` (page buttons, nav module entries via manifest `permission`); client editors fetch `/api/admin/pages/perms` for capability flags.
- Cross-cutting guards: `assertProtectedUserWouldRemain` (transactional last-admin invariant on delete/demote/self-delete), `canActOnUser` (only admins act on protected-role users).

### Admin UI

Navigation (defined in `components/admin/AdminNav.tsx`): Dashboard; then any ungrouped module nav entries (no `navGroupLabel` - currently just contact-form's Inbox); Content → Pages, Menus, Media; System → Users, Styles, Layouts, Modules, Settings; then labelled module nav groups (own named section, e.g. Gazette, Boards); footer: My Account, Sign out, version. Sidebar collapses to a rail (auto-collapses inside Puck editors), mobile drawer with backdrop; toolbar has collapse toggle, ThemeToggle, NotificationBell. When collapsed, each icon link shows a custom hover/focus tooltip to its right (label text) instead of the native `title`: a `createPortal`-to-`<body>` fixed-positioned `.admin-nav-tip` (visuals match `.theme-toggle-tip`), because the nav scroll container's `overflow-x: hidden` would clip a pure-CSS tooltip; collapsed links also carry `aria-label` for the accessible name. Each labelled section is independently collapsible (click the label, chevron flips) - state persisted per-label in `localStorage` (`cactus-sidebar-sections-collapsed`), defaults to all sections maximised; only visible when the rail itself isn't collapsed. There is no standalone Members section, People section, or Roles link any more (all removed in an admin-UI reorganisation - see below and the top-of-file changelog); Users lives in System now.

Members/Roles/Users admin surface has been consolidated (previously a permission-filtered **Members** sidebar section per Phase 5 of MEMBERS_SPEC.md, plus a standalone `/cactus-admin/roles` page) - the section/page are gone; every permission gate that used to guard a nav entry now guards a tab instead:

- `app/cactus-admin/page.tsx` (main dashboard) - the former Members Overview counts (total/active/pending-verification/pending-approval/suspended/scheduled-for-deletion) now render as extra stat tiles alongside Pages/Users/Media, queried only when the viewer holds `members.list`.
- `app/cactus-admin/users/page.tsx` - a server component reading `?tab=` (href-based `TabStrip`, default `users`): **Users** (`PeopleListClient.tsx`, unified staff+member table, unconditional), **Pending Approval** (`PendingApprovalClient.tsx`, gated `members.approve`), **Invites** (`InvitesClient.tsx`, gated `members.invite`). The former standalone **Members** tab was merged into Users (`MembersListClient.tsx` deleted) - a Member row's Type badge/Role-or-status column comes from the same `GET /api/admin/people` call as staff rows. `lib/members/admin-notify.ts`'s pending-approval alert links to `/users?tab=pending-approval`.
- `app/cactus-admin/config/ConfigPageClient.tsx` (Settings) - GDPR & Legal tab gained `MembersGdprClient.tsx` (was `members/gdpr/GdprClient.tsx`) rendered inline at the bottom, gated `members.gdpr`, showing the same pending-deletions/exports/consent/processing-log content plus any `members.gdpr-entry` extension contributions. A **Users** tab (only shown when the viewer holds at least one of `members.settings`/`roles.manage`/`members.email-templates`) holds Registration/Avatars/Usernames/Account sections/Access control (`MembersSettingsTab.tsx`), Roles (`RolesClient.tsx`), Email templates (`EmailTemplatesClient.tsx`) as state-driven subtabs, each only shown/rendered when its own permission is held - see the Admin UI section below for the current subtab layout.
- `app/cactus-admin/members/` now holds only `[id]/` (`MemberDetailClient.tsx` - edit profile, status actions, sessions, reset-password, export-trigger, append-only notes, action log, admin delete, `members.admin-member-detail` extension point) - unchanged.

No permission keys, API routes, or DB schema changed in this reorganisation - every `members.*`/`roles.manage` check still gates exactly what it used to, just relocated.

Pages and routes: listed in the Routes section above.

Settings tabs (`/cactus-admin/config`):

- General: siteName, tagline, description, homepageId, mainMenuId, timezone (9 options), dateFormat, timeFormat, adminPath, trustDeviceDays (1–365); core-updates panel (channel toggle, check, update-now with optional module bundling); Danger zone (Reset Database soft/hard, Reset Everything for Vercel env vars). (Refresh Starter Templates button removed - starter templates auto-refresh after core updates via `ensureStarterLayoutsCurrent`.)
- Branding: logo (+dark), a one-shot **App icon** source upload that auto-generates favicon/apple/PWA icons, per-slot overrides, and app name/short-name/theme+background colour fields (`BrandingImageField` + inline inputs in `ConfigPageClient.tsx` - preview/replace/remove, posts to `/api/admin/media`, stores returned ids on the matching `config.*MediaId`, persisted by the top "Save changes"). App-icon flow: `handleAppIconUploaded` stores the source then POSTs `{sourceMediaId}` to `POST /api/admin/branding/generate-icons` (`media.upload`; sharp resizes to favicon 96 / apple-touch 180 opaque-white / PWA 192 / 512, stores each via `uploadMedia`+`saveMediaRecord`, returns ids+urls) and drops them into `faviconMediaId`/`appleTouchIconMediaId`/`webManifest192MediaId`/`webManifest512MediaId` (each still hand-replaceable). Favicon/icon/app-name metadata now resolved site-wide at the root layout + `app/manifest.ts` (see `app/layout.tsx`), not in `app/(public)/layout.tsx` (its favicon `generateMetadata` was removed). Dark logo swaps in on the frontend via CSS `img[data-logo-variant]` rules in `globals.css` keyed on `data-theme`; dark favicon is emitted as a second `prefers-color-scheme: dark` icon. All dark + app-icon fields optional. Gated on real media state (`config.mediaProvider` set AND `envKeysForProvider(provider).every(k => envStatus[k])`, mirroring the server upload gate); shows the "configure a media provider first" note only when that gate is false. Accepts JPEG/PNG/WebP/GIF/SVG (server `ALLOWED_TYPES` in `lib/media/upload.ts`). This branding UI actually now lives in `BrandingTab.tsx` under `/appearance/styles`, not `ConfigPageClient.tsx`. Object-key extension for an upload is derived from its MIME subtype (`extensionForMimeType`, `lib/media/upload.ts`) with the `+xml`/`+json` RFC 6839 suffix stripped - a raw split previously produced keys like `…-favicon.svg+xml`, and the literal `+` broke the Cloudflare Worker's B2 fetch/signing (confirmed 502 in production; plain-extension PNGs served fine). `BrandingImageField` previews now show an inline "Image not found" state (`onError` on the `<img>`) instead of a broken-image icon when a stored file can't load. Below the icon upload fields, `IconPreviewGallery` renders illustrative mock-ups (browser tab, iPhone/Android home screen, installed-app splash) built from whichever icons are currently staged, so a non-technical owner can see where each generated size actually shows up. Logo field only (`allowOptimise` prop): an **Optimise** button `POST`s `config.logoMediaId` to `/api/admin/media/optimise` and, on success, swaps the logo to the returned lighter media id + shows a `240 KB → 38 KB (84% smaller)` note (`formatBytes` helper); "already about as small as it gets" when no gain.
- Email: emailFromName, emailFromAddress; Brevo/SMTP credential cards writing to Vercel env vars.
- Media: provider select (grouped Proxied/Direct, saved immediately), per-provider env-var checklist + CLOUDFLARE_WORKER_URL for proxied, per-provider media breakdown, client-driven migration with progress/cancel/retry.
- Site Status: status select (live/comingSoon/maintenance), hideFromCrawlers, link to statusPage layouts.
- GDPR & Legal: privacyPolicyPageId, termsPageId, privacy-generator link, sessionPurgeAfterDays, recoveryPurgeAfterDays, cookie-consent banner editor (enable, style, copy fields, category table with pinned "necessary", module-suggested categories, reConsentDays, consentLogRetentionDays, categoriesVersion display); below all of that, if the viewer holds `members.gdpr`, `MembersGdprClient.tsx` renders Members-specific GDPR data (pending deletions, exports, consent records, processing log) plus `members.gdpr-entry` extension contributions.
- Integrations: GitHub App connect/install/disconnect card; env-var cards for Edge Config, Turnstile, Vercel webhook, Sentry, Neon.
- Users (conditional - only shown when the viewer holds `members.settings`, `roles.manage`, or `members.email-templates`): a second, state-driven `TabStrip`, defaulting to the first subtab the viewer can see. The old wrapping "Members" subtab is gone - `MembersSettingsTab.tsx` no longer owns its own nested `TabStrip`; instead it takes the active subtab as a `tab` prop (`MembersSettingsTabKey`), and its five subtabs (Registration, Avatars, Usernames, Account sections, Access control - all gated `members.settings`) are promoted to sit directly in the outer `TabStrip`, in the slot the single "Members" tab used to occupy (i.e. before Roles/Email templates). Roles (`RolesClient.tsx`, gated `roles.manage`, same role picker + permission matrix as the former standalone `/cactus-admin/roles` page, `core.roles-page` extension point still rendered beneath it), Email templates (`EmailTemplatesClient.tsx`, gated `members.email-templates`, same template picker/editor).
- Module tabs: rendered generically, appended after the core tabs (and after Users, when shown), one per `settingsTabs` entry in an active module's manifest (permission-filtered server-side, same gating as `navEntries`). Currently: `contact-form-reply-catcher` ("Reply Catcher", tab id `contact-form-reply-catcher`) - mailbox provider (IMAP/Outlook OAuth), credentials, folder overrides, last-poll status, check-now, OAuth connect; `gazette` ("Gazette", tab id `gazette`, `GazetteSettingsTab.tsx`) - posts-per-page, RSS feed title/description, comments (enable/visibility/moderation/threading), reactions (enable + emoji set), with the WordPress/Medium/Substack import wizard appended below as its own section, replacing the former standalone `/cactus-admin/m/gazette/settings` and `/cactus-admin/m/gazette/import` pages.

Settings keys stored in the database = the SiteConfig columns (types and defaults listed in the Database Schema section). `designTokens` (Json) holds the v2 design-token object (defaults in `lib/design/tokens.ts:DEFAULT_DESIGN_TOKENS`: primary #2c7558/#459578, secondary white/#0f172a, system-ui font, heading sizes 2.5rem→1rem, link colours, status accents info #3b82f6 / success #16a34a / warning #f59e0b / error #ef4444 with brighter dark siblings, blockPadding 1.5rem, tabletBreakpoint 1024px, mobileBreakpoint 640px). `consentBannerConfig` (Json) holds `ConsentBannerConfig` (defaults in `lib/consent/types.ts`: disabled, bottom-bar, four categories necessary/preferences/analytics/marketing, reConsentDays 365, retention null, versions 0).

Client-side storage keys used by the admin: `localStorage cactus-theme`, `localStorage cactus-sidebar-collapsed`, `sessionStorage cactus-core-update-check`, `sessionStorage cactus-module-update-check-<id>` (both 10-minute throttles).

Credentials/env vars are never stored in the database; they are written to Vercel project env vars via `/api/admin/env` (read-only display in local mode).

### Puck Integration

- Library: `@puckeditor/core` ^0.22. Editor components (`<Puck>`) are client-only, lazy-loaded with `ssr: false`; public rendering uses `<Render>` from `@puckeditor/core/rsc`.
- **Custom field widgets reach `config.tsx` through a registry, never a direct import** (`lib/puck/fields/registry.tsx` + `lib/puck/fields/editor.ts`). The 14 sidebar widgets are all `'use client'` and `ResponsiveValueField` imports the Puck editor entrypoint, so importing one from `config.tsx` (which has no `'use client'`) opens a client boundary in the RSC graph and drags the whole editor, plus its vendored TipTap/ProseMirror, into every public page's bundle. `registry.tsx` exports server-safe proxies typed via `import type` (erased, no runtime edge); `editor.ts` (`'use client'`) holds the only real imports and is imported solely by `PuckEditor.tsx` / `LayoutPuckEditor.tsx`, which call `registerEditorFields()` at module scope. The same registry also carries the RichTextBlock `renderMenu` renderer (`RichTextMenuWithLink`), not just sidebar field widgets, for the same bundle-isolation reason - it imports the Puck editor runtime. `lib/puck/fields/registry.test.ts` fails if the two lists drift or if anyone reinstates a direct import - without it a missing registration renders the field as nothing, silently.
- Central config: `lib/puck/config.tsx` (safe for both editor and RSC paths; no hooks/browser APIs). Exports: `puckConfig` (default, full-page editor), `puckRscConfig`, `footerPuckConfig(+Rsc)`, `layoutPuckConfig(+Rsc)` (adds `ContentSlot`), `headerPuckConfig(+Rsc)`, `fullPagePuckConfig(+Rsc)` (aliases of puckConfig). RSC variants swap `SiteLogo` to an RSC renderer and replace the `richtext` field type with textarea (TipTap JSON is converted to HTML via `@tiptap/html` for RSC rendering).
- Root ("nothing selected") fields, right sidebar: `puckConfig.root` (pages) and `headerPuckConfig.root`/`footerPuckConfig.root` define real fields, rendered via each config's own `root.render`. `puckConfig.root` gained `bg` (`PageBgColorField`, none/colour) and `paddingY` (none/sm/md/lg, padding above the first Section and below the last) - deliberately no page-level `maxWidth`, since every `Section` already owns its own maxWidth/full-bleed background and a shared root wrapper would clip it. `layoutPuckConfig.root` and `getModuleLayoutPuckConfig(type).root` still define no fields, so Puck falls back to its built-in `{title: text}` root field (`@puckeditor/core`'s `defaultPageFields`) - which would duplicate the Title/Name field our own Settings tab already owns, so `LayoutPuckEditor.tsx` passes `overrides={{fields: hideRootFieldsOverride}}` (`lib/puck/tabs/rootFieldsOverride.tsx`) whenever the active config has no `root.fields`, hiding just the field body (Puck always renders the "Page" breadcrumb header regardless). `PuckEditor.tsx` (pages) needs no such override since `puckConfig.root.fields` is always real.
- Core blocks by category - Layout: Section (background/overlay/padding/max-width/sticky/border/shadow/opacity + slot; `bgType: 'grid-scan'` renders a decorative graph-paper grid + looping scan-beam sweep behind nested content, purely cosmetic; **outer `overflow` is now conditional** - only `hidden` when the section actually clips to an edged box (borderRadius≠none, bg image, overlay scrim, boxShadow, grid-scan), otherwise `visible` so a `position:sticky` descendant - e.g. a sticky image column inside a nested Grid - isn't trapped by an overflow context it doesn't need), Grid2/Grid3/Grid4 (fixed-column-count variants, ratios, per-column align/width, `stackColumns` mobile|tablet|never - `GridBlock` derives a `stackMode` from it (falling back to the legacy `stackAtTablet:'on'`→tablet, else `mobile` for a normal grid / `never` for one already managing its own per-breakpoint columns) and emits `data-stack="<mode>"` on every grid; `buildTokenStyles` keys the collapse rules off it - `mobile` stacks to one column at the mobile breakpoint (with the 3/4→2-col tablet step), `tablet` stacks across the whole tablet band and below, `never` holds the columns at every width. The stack rules outrank a grid's own scoped `[data-grid-id]` override, so an explicit stack choice stacks even a Manual-width grid. Per-column widths (`col{n}Width`) now only apply in Manual `columnSizes` mode (per breakpoint), so switching the preset back to Equal drops stale custom widths immediately instead of a lingering width silently winning, per-column `col{n}Sticky` off|on + `col{n}StickyOffset` - `on` pins that column's grid track (`position:sticky`, `top:offset`, `align-self:start` so the box stays content-height inside the full-height row and has room to travel) while the taller sibling scrolls; the track carries `data-col-sticky` and the block emits media rules dropping it back to `position:static` once the grid stacks (per `stackMode`: mobile band when `mobile`/`tablet`, plus the tablet band when `tablet`; never when `never`), so a pinned image just sits in normal flow on small screens. NB the sticky must live on the track div itself, not a nested block wrapped in a Section: the per-block visibility/slot wrapper between the track and a nested block is content-height, which caps a sticky descendant's travel to zero, per-column "scale to width" (wraps that column's content in `lib/puck/components/ScaleToFit.tsx` - a client component that measures natural size + applies `transform:scale(min(1,colWidth/naturalWidth))` so any content, incl. fixed-size icon widgets like ThemeToggle/cart, shrinks to fit; transform-origin follows `col*Align`) - **no longer its own field**: `GridBlock` derives it (`colScaled`) from whether that column's `col*WidthShrunk` has a value, since a column's rendered width only ever changes at runtime via the shrink-on-scroll override; the standalone `col*Scale` radio (Grid2/3/4 and the legacy dynamic `Grid`) was removed, 2/3/4 slots respectively - split from a single dynamic "Grid" so Puck's Outline panel only ever lists the slots that variant actually has; legacy dynamic `Grid` stays registered as a safety net but is unlisted in every picker), Group (flex row/column + slot; gained `columns` responsive select auto|1-6 (`ResponsiveSelectField`) - `auto`/blank keeps the default flex-wrap flow (every legacy Group byte-identical), a number switches the slot wrapper to an equal-width CSS grid `repeat(N, minmax(0,1fr))` that reflows per breakpoint via `responsiveMediaCssFor` on the same `.group-rsp-<id>` class, so an arbitrary child count sits N-per-row and can differ desktop/tablet/mobile (e.g. 3/2/1) - the flow the fixed-track Grid2/3/4 can't do since they cap at 4 one-child tracks and orphan the odd item when a 3-track grid drops to 2 at tablet; grid branch skips the header-centring `nth-child` style), Split (ratio columns, legacy zones/DropZone API not slot fields), Spacer, Divider. Typography: Heading (gained `revealAnimation: 'none'|'stagger-lines'` - splits `text` on `\n` into per-line clipped spans that rise in on mount, independent of the existing scroll-triggered `aosFields` also on this block; `text` field is `textarea` to allow multi-line entry; `level` gained a `display` option - the largest level, above h2, renders as a real `<h1>` with a `cactus-display` class, styled from `themeStyle.display` tokens; also gained `highlightText` + `highlightMark` - `highlightText` is a substring that gets recoloured in `--color-primary` and wrapped in a non-italic `<em>`, and when `highlightMark: 'underline'` also carries a chunky mustard bar sitting UNDER the word (a thick `text-decoration: underline`, 0.16em / `skip-ink: none` / small offset - deliberately under the glyphs not behind them, and a solid `--color-heading-mark` token / `#E3A857` fallback rather than a translucent one so a tinted hero background can't bleed through and turn it olive) (works inside `stagger-lines` too, applied per line via the shared `renderHighlight` helper); also gained a swatch/manual colour picker (`color` is now `SiteColourField allowManual` - swatch/custom/None/typed CSS colour, legacy `dark`/`muted`/`brand` still resolve, empty = per-level heading token), whole-heading linking (`href` wraps the tag in a colour-inheriting block `<a data-heading-link>`), an optional hover underline on linked headings (`hoverUnderline` yes/no + `hoverUnderlineColor` swatch, scoped `<style>` on the id, defaults to `currentColor`), and vertical positioning (`minHeight` none/sm 240/md 400/lg 600/screen 100vh + `verticalAlign` top/middle/bottom - a set height makes the wrapper a flex column and drops the tag's bottom margin so centring is true); also gained `fitOneLine` ("Keep on one line (shrink text to fit)", no/yes, default no) - wraps the heading's content in `lib/puck/components/HeadingFitText.tsx`, a client component that measures the text's natural one-line width against the room the heading has and scales it down to fit, bringing the box height down with it; the Menu block's `fitOneLine` trick, see the dated notes at the top), TextBlock (gained `size` base/md/lg, `maxWidth` none/prose 46ch/wide 60ch and `color` secondary/muted/dark - defaults preserve the old full-width secondary-colour 1rem look; used together they turn a plain paragraph into a constrained "lede" that wraps to multiple lines like the concept), RichTextBlock (TipTap), Quote (quote/attribution/padding + optional photo; the photo is now rendered INSIDE the `<blockquote>` - first child of a flex row that also holds the text, so it sits between the left accent border and the quote - where it used to be a sibling `<img>` to the left of the whole panel, outside it. `imageSize` sets the photo's width (sm 72 / md 112 / lg 160), new `imageHeight` number field overrides its height in px (blank or 0 = square, i.e. the old behaviour; a circle shape with an unequal height renders as an ellipse, which is the point of asking), `imageShape` circle/rounded/square. All photo fields stay hidden by `resolveFields` until `mediaUrl` is set), Caption (text/align/padding, styled from `themeStyle.caption` tokens via a `cactus-caption` class - small label/footnote text usable anywhere, not just form-field labels). Actions: ButtonLink (label/href/variant/align/padding, plus six Custom-only props; 2026-07-14: `variant` gained a fourth option `custom` alongside primary/secondary/outline. The three presets take their colours from the Styles → Buttons design tokens; `custom` ignores those and paints from the block's own `bgColor`/`textColor`/`hoverBgColor`/`hoverTextColor` (each a `SiteColourField` - palette swatches + native colour picker + free-text CSS colour) and `borderWidth` (`BUTTON_BORDER_OPTIONS`: none/1px/2px/3px/4px) with `borderColor`. Any custom colour left blank falls back to the matching primary token, so a freshly-switched custom button is identical to the primary it came from; a border width chosen with no colour picked paints `currentColor`, never transparent. `resolveFields` strips all six colour/border props unless `variant === 'custom'`, and strips `borderColor` until a width is picked, so only applicable options show. Hover for `custom` is a block-scoped `a[data-btn-link="<id>"]:hover{…!important}` rule emitted by the block itself - the global hover rules in `lib/design/tokens.ts` are keyed on `[data-variant="primary"|"secondary"|"outline"]` and deliberately never match `custom`; `!important` beats the inline base style, same reason those rules carry it. `align` (2026-07-14) is a responsive select (`ResponsiveSelectField`, left/center/right) emitting `text-align` on the wrapper `div[data-btn-id]` via `responsiveMediaCssFor`, with the `<a>` staying `display:inline-block`; blank resolves to `inherit`, which for an inherited property is the same as declaring nothing, so buttons saved before the field existed keep taking their container's alignment rather than being yanked left), Phone (2026-07-15, `PhoneBlock` - click-to-call number. Registered in `puckConfig` (page/infopage), `layoutPuckConfig` (infoPage + generic layouts, in the `actions` category), `headerPuckConfig` (`actions` category) and `footerPuckConfig` (`site` category, `noGutterDefault`) - so it appears in the page/infopage editor and in every layout-editor type (header/footer/infoPage/statusPage/generic), not just the plain layout config. RSC parity automatic via the shared render + the `...components` spreads in `puckRscConfig`/`layoutPuckRscConfig`/`headerPuckRscConfig`/`footerPuckRscConfig`. `number` free-text (kept legible with spaces/brackets) is stripped to `[\d+]` with a single leading `+` for the `tel:` href; optional `label` overrides the displayed text (blank shows the number). `showIcon` none|mobile|always injects an inline phone SVG - `mobile` hides it by default and un-hides under `mobileMediaQuery()` via a block-scoped `[data-phone-id]` style. `mobileIconOnly` no|yes (2026-07-15): when the icon shows on phones, drops the number text under `mobileMediaQuery()` (a `[data-phone-text]{display:none}` rule) so only the dial glyph remains on mobile - the `<a>`'s `aria-label` still carries the number so taps and screen readers keep it; hidden by `resolveFields` unless `showIcon` puts an icon on mobile. Full typography set to recreate a heading-styled number: `align` responsive select, `size` sm/base/md/lg/xl/xxl (`PHONE_SIZE_MAP`), `weight` normal/medium/semibold/bold (`PHONE_WEIGHT_MAP`), `transform` none/uppercase/capitalize/lowercase, `letterSpacing` (`UnitValueField` em/px), `fontFamily` (`SiteFontField`, non-system Google families hoisted via `googleFontHrefForFamily()` + `<link precedence>`), `color`/`hoverColor` (`SiteColourField allowManual`). Underline: `underline` no|yes (base) and `hoverUnderline` ''(no change)|underline|none, with shared `underlineColor` + `underlineThickness` + `underlineOffset` (`UnitValueField`) that `resolveFields` shows when EITHER base or hover underline is on (so a hover-only underline - the common "underline the number when you point at it" look - can still be fully styled). **The underline is painted on the number `[data-phone-text]` span, not the `<a>`** (2026-07-15 fix): the `<a>` is pinned to `text-decoration:none !important` and the span carries `text-decoration-line/color/thickness/offset`, because the global `a:hover{text-decoration:underline}` in globals.css was re-underlining the link on hover at the browser's default thickness and wiping out a chosen thickness/colour (and decoration on the inline-flex link didn't reach the text reliably). Hover toggles the span's decoration via `a[data-phone-link]:hover [data-phone-text]{…}`; hover colour stays on the link (`:hover{color…!important}`). `fitOneLine` no|yes (2026-07-15) wraps the icon+number in `HeadingFitText` (same client shrink-to-fit as the Heading/Menu blocks; link is `display:block` so it has a full width to measure against). Vertical positioning (2026-07-15) mirrors Heading: `minHeight` (`BLOCK_HEIGHT_OPTIONS` incl. fill/screen, responsive) + `verticalAlign` top/middle/bottom turn the wrapper into a flex column (`PHONE_VALIGN_MAP`), desktop inline + tablet/mobile via `responsiveMediaCssFor` on `[data-phone-id]`, `blockFillCssResponsive` for fill; `verticalAlign` hidden by `resolveFields` until a height is set. **Icon visibility is stylesheet-only** (2026-07-15 fix): the icon span carries NO inline `display` - `showIcon: mobile` sets `display:none` at base + `inline-flex` under `mobileMediaQuery()`; an earlier inline `display:none` outranked the media rule so the icon never appeared on phones. `mobileIconOnly` yes drops `[data-phone-text]` under the mobile breakpoint so only the glyph shows (aria-label keeps the number). Plus the standard padding/sticky/aos/visibility fields), CTABanner. Media: ImageBlock, VideoEmbed (YouTube/Vimeo), Embed (iframe). Content: Hero, Eyebrow (pill label + optional pulsing dot; pill shape now `var(--radius-pill, 9999px)` instead of a hardcoded `9999`, shared with Badge), Card, ImageChipPanel (single `<img>` + a repeatable `chips` array field, each rendered via the standalone `Chip` component at one of 5 corner positions - deliberately an array field rather than a Puck slot, since Puck wraps each slot child in its own drag-handle `_DropZone-item` box which breaks a Chip's `position:absolute` in the editor canvas even though it renders correctly live; array-field items have no such wrapper so this block is WYSIWYG-correct in both; gained a "holo frame" set of settings - `framePadding` (none/sm/md/lg inner gutter that insets the `<img>` and rounds it to `calc(panelRadius - 6px)`), `frameBg` (none/subtle/gradient panel fill behind the inset image), `gridPattern` (reuses the Section block's `cactus-section-grid-scan` graph-paper background) and `scanEffect` (reuses `cactus-section-scan-beam` looping sweep) - the image carries no z-index so the grid stays in the background and the scan beam + chips paint over it via DOM order), Callout (info/success/warning/error boxes - colours read the `--status-{key}`/`-bg`/`-title` vars from Styles → Colours → Status boxes, falling back to the original built-in hexes), Badge (blue/yellow/red/gray colours read `--badge-{key}-bg`/`-text` from Styles → Colours → Badges, falling back to the original hardcoded pastel hexes; `primary` option unchanged, still `--color-primary-subtle`; pill shape now `var(--radius-pill, 9999px)` instead of a hardcoded `9999`), Trustline (repeatable icon+text row, 6 built-in icons), Chip (small label+value card, static-in-flow or floating over a `position:relative` parent via 5 corner presets - fine as a freestanding block, but composing several as siblings inside a `Section`'s image slot is the broken pattern ImageChipPanel replaces), Accordion, FeatureList (gained `iconStyle` emoji|glyph - `glyph` swaps the leading emoji for a 46px solid `--color-primary` rounded square holding a white line-icon from the new `GLYPH_ICONS` map (share/tag/compass/check/shield/clock/star/truck, selected per-item via `item.icon`) and renders larger Fraunces `<h3>` titles + 48ch body; `emoji` default is byte-identical to before; `.cactus-feature-glyph-row` in globals.css adds a hover lift), SpecPanel (windowed "spec sheet" card - dot title-bar + `rows` array field of `{label, value, highlight?, badge?}`; `highlight: 'true'` renders the value in bold `--color-primary`, `badge` renders a green `--color-success` pill; reuses ImageChipPanel's shadow/radius knobs), Ticker (full-bleed teal marquee band - `items` array of `{text}` + `speed` slow/normal/fast; items are duplicated in render and the `.cactus-ticker` class scrolls to `translateX(-50%)` for a seamless loop via the `cactus-ticker` keyframe, Fraunces phrases with mustard `·` separators; respects the global reduced-motion block), Stats, Logos, SocialLinks. Site: SiteHeader (gained `alignment` field - left/center/space-between/space-around - to control horizontal menu item alignment when wrapping to multiple lines; gained the full MenuBlock nav-styling set for its built-in menu: `itemFontFamily` (SiteFontField), `hoverColor`/`hoverBackground`, `activeColor`/`activeFontWeight`/`activeUnderline`(+colour/thickness/offset, extras hidden via `resolveFields` unless underline on) and `showDropdowns` hover|click - all passed through to `MenuBlockClient`), SiteLogo, Copyright, MenuBlock (gained `alignment` field - left/center/space-between/space-around - to control horizontal menu item alignment when wrapping to multiple lines; gained 3 fluid min/max fields - `itemSpacingFluid`/`letterSpacingFluid`/`itemFontSizeFluid`, each `{min, max}` plain text inputs rendered side-by-side by the new `MinMaxPairField` custom Puck field - built into a `clamp(min, preferred, max)` via `fluidClamp()` (`lib/puck/responsiveValue.ts`) that hits `min` at the site's mobile breakpoint and `max` at its tablet breakpoint, continuously shrinking item gap/letter-spacing/font-size as the viewport narrows so a horizontal menu can stay on one line instead of wrapping; empty min/max falls back to the existing `spacing`/`itemFontSize` presets untouched; applied in `MenuBlock`'s vertical branch, `MenuBlockClient` (horizontal, live), and `MenuBlockEditorPreview` (both orientations) for editor/live parity; gained `hoverColor`, `activeColor`, `activeUnderline` (none|underline) + `activeUnderlineColor` (`SiteColourField` swatches; underline-colour field hidden via `resolveFields` unless underline on) - active = exact-path match (`isActiveHref` in `MenuBlockClient.tsx`, relative hrefs only, trailing-slash/query/hash normalised) detected client-side via `usePathname`, active links carry `aria-current="page"`; underline is `text-decoration` 2px thickness / 4px offset, taking the text colour when no separate underline colour set; vertical menus route each anchor through the exported `MenuVerticalLink` client component so hover/active work there too, since the RSC branch can't know the path; gained `itemFontFamily` (new `SiteFontField` custom field - site fonts from Appearance → Styles listed first under "Your fonts" via new cached `useSiteFonts` hook, then the Google Fonts catalogue searchable, or any typed CSS font-family value; empty inherits the site font) - non-system Google families load via a React-hoisted `<link rel="stylesheet" precedence="default">` built by new `googleFontHrefForFamily()` in `lib/design/tokens.ts` (wght 400-700), emitted from `MenuBlockClient`, the vertical RSC branch and the editor preview, so a font picked only on the block still loads without being in the site tokens; `POPULAR_FONTS`/`MAX_FONT_SEARCH_RESULTS` moved from the Styles page into shared `lib/design/font-options.ts`; audit fixes: "Dropdowns open on" now actually works - `showDropdowns` reaches `MenuBlockClient` and `click` mode toggles dropdowns on click (parent-with-children click prevents navigation, closes on outside mousedown via a per-item document listener) instead of hover; `itemColor` converted from free-text to `SiteColourField` swatches (matches SiteHeader, dark-mode-safe); new `hoverBackground` swatch field replaces the hardcoded `--color-primary-subtle` hover pill (which stays as the fallback), wiring up the previously-dead prop; new `activeFontWeight` select ('' = same as items) and `activeUnderlineThickness`/`activeUnderlineOffset` text fields (bare numbers treated as px via `cssLen()`, defaults 2px/4px, hidden with the underline extras); editors now pass `alignment` to `MenuBlockEditorPreview` so the canvas honours it like the live site), LoginButton, ThemeToggle (gained a `style` select - `segmented` icon pill (default), `expand` icon+hover menu, `dropdown` icon+click menu, `text` label pill, `switch` sun/moon two-state slider, `cycle` single icon click-to-step - passed to `ThemeToggleClient`), CookieSettingsLink. Members (MEMBERS_SPEC.md Phase 7): `MembersLogin`/`MembersRegister` (embed the real login/register client forms inline anywhere), `MembersAccountLink` (sign-in/register ↔ my-account/sign-out, the header-friendly member equivalent of `LoginButton` - also registered in `headerPuckConfig`), `MemberGate`/`TrustedMemberGate` (slot-field gates - any member vs `member.trusted`), `MembersProfile` (viewer's own avatar/name/bio). Editor renders always show a fixed preview (no member session to check under an admin editing session); live rendering is async Server Components in `lib/puck/components/MembersBlocksRsc.tsx` (`await connection()` then `getMemberFromCookie()`), swapped in via `rscComponents`/`layoutPuckRscConfig`/`headerPuckRscConfig` - kept out of `config.tsx` itself so the `next/headers`-dependent import chain never reaches the editor's client bundle. Modules category is populated from generated `lib/puck/module-components.ts` (currently: `ContactForm`).
- `headerPuckConfig` block palette (2026-07-13, ImageBlock added 2026-07-15): beyond the chrome/structure blocks (SiteLogo, MenuBlock, LoginButton, ThemeToggle, MembersAccountLink, Grid2/3/4, Group, Spacer, Divider) the header editor now also offers Heading, TextBlock, RichTextBlock (Text category), ButtonLink (Actions category) and ImageBlock (new Media category) - so an owner can put a phone number, strapline, "Call us" button or a logo/badge image in the header. These are static content blocks pulled straight from `puckConfig.components`; `headerPuckRscConfig` picks them up automatically via its `...headerPuckConfig.components` spread (no RSC data override needed, unlike SiteLogo/MembersAccountLink), so editor/frontend markup stays identical.
- `footerPuckConfig` gained a Media category (2026-07-15) holding `ImageBlock` (wrapped in `noGutterDefault` like the footer's other static content blocks, since the footer root already applies its own 1.5rem gutter) - previously the footer editor had no way to place a standalone image at all (only `SiteLogo`).
