Admin pages (`/cactus-admin/m/directory/…`): `entries` (list - `EntriesScreen.tsx`; skeleton-row loading state, result count + "Clear filters", clickable rows open the editor, ⚠️ flag on rows missing lat/lng, `?category=` query param preselects the category filter for deep-links from Categories), `entries/new` / `entries/[id]` (editor - `EntryEditor.tsx`, embeds the module-private Puck config for the description field; transient "Saved ✓" confirmation, error banner auto-scrolls into view, "View live ↗" link once published, preview-link button shows "Link copied ✓"), `entries/import` (CSV wizard - `CsvImport.tsx`, redirects to the entries list if `csv_import_enabled` is off; drag-and-drop drop zone plus a "Download example CSV" template button, "Choose another file"/"Import another file" resets, post-import "View entries" link), `categories` (`CategoriesScreen.tsx` - drag-to-reorder plus ↑/↓ buttons as a non-drag alternative, entry count links through to the entries list filtered to that category). No modal/overlay system used anywhere except the multi-select image picker (`EntryImagesField.tsx`, generalises core's `MediaPickerField.tsx` single-select overlay pattern) - everything else is inline-edit-in-table, matching Boards/Gazette convention.

Public pages (`/directory/…`, via the core `publicBasePath` mechanism): index (category grid + full map + "All listings" heading with a result count + paginated flat list, featured pinned first), `[category]` (category page - breadcrumb back to the directory index, collapsible filtered map, area filter, sort incl. route-marker order when any entry has one set, client-side keyword search with a live result count; 404s if the category has zero published entries, independent of any area-filter result), `[category]/[slug]` (entry detail - breadcrumb trail, gallery/cover with real `alt` text, Puck-rendered description, contact card with a `tel:` link for phone, single-pin location map plus a "Get directions ↗" link to Google Maps (coords if set, else the address), tag chips; 404s on missing/wrong-category/draft), `preview/[token]` (hash lookup, `noindex`, renders regardless of status with a warning banner - Gazette's preview-page pattern verbatim). Breadcrumb/section-heading/result-count styling lives in shared `.dir-breadcrumb`/`.dir-section-heading`/`.dir-result-count` classes in `DirectoryStyles.tsx`.

**Extension Points**
- `core.admin-dashboard-widgets` (id `directory-summary`) - dashboard summary widget.
- `core.menu-entity-provider` (id `directory`, `lib/menu-entity-provider.ts` → `directoryMenuEntityProvider`) - lets the admin Menus builder link to a category or a listing.

**Puck Blocks**

- No manifest-registered `puckBlocks` (nothing site-embeddable, unlike Gazette's `GazetteFeed`/`GazetteFeatured`).
- Module-private only (not in the manifest, only used inside the entry editor's own embedded Puck config and the public/preview RSC render): `DirectoryProse` - one block, richtext only (heading levels 2-4, code/codeBlock/strike/underline/horizontalRule/textAlign all disabled), same minimal single-block shape as Gazette/Boards' own prose blocks but with no pull-quote/code/image/divider siblings, since the spec only calls for one rich-text field per entry.

**Configuration**
Global, in the `dir_settings` singleton row (see Database), edited via the "Directory" tab on core `/cactus-admin/config` (`DirectorySettingsTab.tsx`, `settingsTabs` manifest entry, `directory.manage`). No `requiredEnvVars` - geocoding needs no API key, just a `User-Agent` header built from the site's own configured name.

**External Integrations**
OpenStreetMap Nominatim (free geocoding, no key, `User-Agent: "<siteName> (Cactus Directory)"` per Nominatim's usage policy), OpenStreetMap tile server (public map tiles, no key), core media (`Media.id` for the ordered `images` array, no FK), `leaflet` + `leaflet.markercluster` (new **core** runtime dependencies - modules compile inside core's Next build so map-rendering deps had to land in core `package.json`, the only core code diff this module needed besides `FIELD_NOTES.md`/wiki, precedent: `shiki` was added the same way for Gazette).

**Cron Jobs**
`0 1 * * *` → `/api/m/directory/cron/expire-featured` (clears `featured`/`featured_until` on any entry whose `featured_until` has passed); registered via `cronJobs` in `cactus.module.json`, emitted into the generated `vercel.json`. `CRON_SECRET` bearer-gated, same pattern as Boards' digest cron.

**Scripts**
None.

**Known Limitations**

- CSV import validation (required fields, lat/lng ranges, email/website format, parseable `featured_until`, duplicate-name-within-file) runs entirely client-side against the parsed file before the "ready" rows are POSTed; the server re-validates via the same zod schema but does not repeat the duplicate-within-file check (a DB-level clash is impossible anyway since `ensureUniqueEntrySlug` auto-suffixes).
- The multi-image picker (`EntryImagesField.tsx`) has no existing multi-select precedent anywhere else in the codebase to follow - it's a from-scratch generalisation of `lib/puck/MediaPickerField.tsx`'s single-select `MediaPickerModal` overlay, not a shared core component.
- `leaflet`/`leaflet.markercluster` default marker icon assets are deliberately not used (they resolve via relative image paths that don't survive Next's bundler without extra webpack config) - pins are plain CSS-coloured `L.divIcon` circles instead, sidestepping the issue entirely rather than configuring asset resolution.

### Shop

- Slug: `shop` (table prefix `shp_`), repo `github.com/cactus-foundation-modules/shop`, manifest version 0.1.21, pinned in `modules.json` to v0.1.21.
- Full ecommerce foundation: catalogue (products - physical/digital/service, categories, tags, collections), checkout with a pluggable payment-provider interface (Stripe, PayPal, bank transfer, cash - all four fully built), orders with per-item refunds and a manual-order-entry route, customers (derived from orders by email, no dedicated table), discounts (coupon codes + priority-ordered automatic discounts), tax (per-zone rates, inclusive/exclusive mode) and shipping (postcode-prefix zones, flat/weight-banded/free rates), back-in-stock email subscriptions, pre-orders, CSV product import/export, and related-products/upsells (manual curation with an automatic same-category fallback). Optional integration with Members (guest checkout always works; saved addresses, order history, post-purchase account prompt when Members is enabled) and Reply Catcher (shop's side of a Customer Communications tab only - see Extension Points).
- Layout system integration (core mechanism, see Puck Integration above - Shop is the 4th module on it, joining Directory/Gazette/Boards): declares `layoutTypes` group "Shop" with seven types - `shopIndex` ("Shop Home"), `shopCategory` ("Category"), `shopCollection` ("Collection"), `shopProduct` ("Product"), `shopCheckout` ("Checkout"), `shopConfirmation` ("Confirmation"), `shopCart` ("Cart", added later when the cart page joined the layout system) - more types than any other module since Shop has more distinct page kinds than a category/entry pair. 2 new blocks in `components/puck/`: `ShopCategoryHeader`, `ShopCollectionHeader` (both `[ANCHOR]`, same shape as `DirectoryCategoryHeader` - re-fetch their own data from an injected slug, nothing else to inject). Existing blocks retagged by page: `ShopProductGrid`/`ShopProductCard` → `shopIndex`+`shopCategory`+`shopCollection` (one grid block reused across all three listing contexts, exactly like Gazette's `gazetteCategory` reuse); `ShopFeaturedCollection`/`ShopCategoryBrowser`/`ShopPromoBanner` → `shopIndex` only; `ShopProductDetail`/`ShopBackInStockForm`/`ShopRelatedProducts` → `shopProduct`; `ShopCheckoutContact`/`Shipping`/`Payment`/`Review` → `shopCheckout`; `ShopUpsellProducts` → `shopProduct` + `shopCheckout` + `shopCart` (later); `ShopOrderConfirmation` → `shopConfirmation`; `ShopCartFull` (later) → `shopCart`. `ShopCartSummary` stays untagged (header-placement mini-cart widget, not part of any of these page types). `lib/inject-category-context.ts`/`lib/inject-collection-context.ts` inject `{categorySlug}`/`{collectionSlug}`; `lib/inject-product-context.ts` (pre-existing) injects `{productSlug, productId, inStock}` - unchanged, just now called from the generic path instead of the retired bespoke one. `lib/starterLayouts.ts` provides 3 starters per type (21 total) - `shopCategory`/`shopCollection` seed all-draft with the pre-existing hardcoded plain-grid pages as fallback (new templating, same principle as Directory/Gazette/Boards); `shopIndex`/`shopProduct`/`shopCheckout`/`shopConfirmation` have **no** hardcoded fallback (they were Puck-only from day one via the old table) so exactly one starter per type sets `publishByDefault: true`, carrying over the old table's default block arrangement so the storefront looks identical to before on first seed. `shopCart` is the hybrid: it KEEPS its hardcoded cart (`CartPageClient`) as a fallback like category/collection, yet still ships one `publishByDefault` starter (Cart block + upsells) so the basket is designable out of the box but can never go blank if the layout is unpublished. This replaced Shop's own pre-existing bespoke mechanism entirely (see "Retired" note under Database below) rather than running the two side by side.

**Database**
Table prefix: `shp_` (30 tables total, incl. addendum). Full DDL in `modules/shop/migrations/001_initial.sql`; later per-change files are numbered (`002_master_category.sql` adds the product master category to existing installs, idempotently).

- `shp_products` - name/slug(unique)/type(PHYSICAL\|DIGITAL\|SERVICE)/status(DRAFT\|ACTIVE\|ARCHIVED)/description/short_description/sku(unique)/barcode, pricing (price/compare_at_price/cost_price/tax_class_id FK), inventory (track_inventory/stock_count/low_stock_threshold/out_of_stock_behaviour BLOCK\|BACKORDER, `low_stock_alerted_at` dedupe marker for the daily cron - cleared on any stock_count write so a restock re-arms it), physical dimensions, digital_file_id FK + download_limit/download_expiry, SEO fields + `og_image_id` (no FK, core Media table), `master_category_id` (FK shp_categories ON DELETE SET NULL - the product's lead category; one per product, drives its media folder path; FK added via `ALTER` after shp_categories exists since it's a forward ref, plus idempotent `migrations/002_master_category.sql` for existing installs), pre-order fields (is_pre_order/pre_order_dispatch_date/pre_order_note/pre_order_max_quantity/pre_order_count), recommendation fields (related_mode/upsell_mode AUTOMATIC\|MANUAL, related_limit/upsell_limit default 4), timestamps.
- `shp_product_media` - product_id FK cascade, type(IMAGE\|VIDEO_FILE\|VIDEO_URL), url, alt_text, position, is_primary.
- `shp_categories` - self-referencing parent_id (**ON DELETE SET NULL** - deleting a parent promotes children to root, unlike Directory's RESTRICT), name/slug(unique)/description/position/SEO fields. `shp_product_categories` join table (no position). A product stays a member of any number of categories here; the single lead one is `shp_products.master_category_id`. `getPrimaryCategoryId()` returns the master when set, else falls back to first membership (used by automatic recommendations).
- `shp_tags` - name/slug both unique. `shp_product_tags` join table.
- `shp_collections` - name/slug(unique)/description/image_id/position/SEO fields. `shp_product_collections` join table (has its own `position` - product order within that collection).
- `shp_tax_classes` (name/code unique), `shp_shipping_zones` (name, postcodes JSONB array of prefixes - not `TEXT[]`, matches Directory/Gazette's existing JSONB-array precedent), `shp_tax_zone_rates` (zone+class unique, rate NUMERIC(5,4)), `shp_shipping_rates` (zone_id FK, type FLAT\|WEIGHT_BASED\|FREE, flat_rate/weight_rates JSONB array of `{upToKg,rate}`/free_threshold/estimated_days/position/is_active).
- `shp_digital_files` (filename/url/size/mime_type) + `shp_digital_downloads` (order_id/order_item_id/file_id FKs, unique `token`, download_count, expires_at).
- `shp_coupons` (code unique, type PERCENTAGE\|FIXED_AMOUNT\|FREE_SHIPPING, value/minimum_order_value/usage_limit/usage_count/per_customer_limit/starts_at/expires_at/is_active) + `shp_automatic_discounts` (same shape minus code/usage tracking, plus free_shipping_threshold/priority).
- `shp_orders` - order_number (unique, generated from a dedicated `shp_order_number_seq` Postgres sequence, not a COUNT(*) scheme, so concurrent checkouts can never collide), status (8-value CHECK), member_id (nullable, no FK - Members is optional), customer snapshot (email/name/phone), shipping_address/billing_address JSONB (`ShpAddress` shape), financials (subtotal/discount_amount/shipping_amount/tax_amount/total/tax_mode snapshot/currency), coupon_id FK + coupon_code snapshot, payment_method/payment_status/payment_reference/paid_at, shipping_rate_id (no FK, snapshot only) + shipping_rate_name.
- `shp_order_items` - order_id FK cascade, product_id FK **SET NULL** (product may later be deleted, snapshot fields survive it), product_name/sku/type snapshot, quantity/unit_price/tax_rate/tax_amount/total, refunded_qty, is_pre_order + pre_order_dispatch_date snapshot.
- `shp_refunds` (order_id FK, amount/reason/provider_refund_id/status/created_by) + `shp_refund_items` (refund_id FK cascade, order_item_id FK restrict, quantity/amount).
- `shp_order_notes` (is_internal flag - false = customer-visible) + `shp_order_emails` (send log: subject/to/sent_at/trigger - `trigger` values incl. `MANUAL` for admin-composed sends and `REPLY_CATCHER` reserved for the extension point).
- `shp_saved_addresses` - member_id (no FK, bare string), label, is_default (single-default enforced app-side in a transaction), address JSONB.
- `shp_email_templates` - trigger(unique)/subject/body_html/is_active. Seeded (INSERT...ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING) with all 9 triggers: `ORDER_CONFIRMED` (has the one `{{#if hasPreOrderItems}}` conditional block the renderer supports), `STATUS_PROCESSING`/`STATUS_SHIPPED`/`STATUS_COMPLETED`/`STATUS_CANCELLED`, `ADMIN_NEW_ORDER`, `LOW_STOCK`, `BACK_IN_STOCK`, `IMPORT_COMPLETE`.
- `shp_back_in_stock_subscriptions` - product_id FK cascade, email, member_id nullable, unique(product_id,email) (idempotent subscribe), notified_at (null = pending, retained after fulfilment for reporting).
- `shp_import_jobs` - status(PENDING\|PROCESSING\|COMPLETED\|FAILED), filename, total/processed/created/updated/skipped row counts, errors JSONB array of `{row,reason}`, column_map JSONB, created_by, started_at/completed_at.
- `shp_related_products`/`shp_upsell_products` (product_id+related_id or product_id+upsell_id composite PK, position, both self-FK cascade to shp_products) + `shp_auto_exclude_products` (per-product exclusions from the automatic-recommendation fallback).
- `shp_settings` - singleton (`id='singleton'`), single `config` JSONB column holding the whole `ShpConfig` blob (Q2 decision - no `shopConfig` column added to core `SiteConfig`, everything lives in this one module-owned row instead).
- **Retired**: `shp_page_layouts` (key(unique: `index`\|`product`\|`checkout`\|`confirmation`)/builder_data JSONB) - the original single-layout-per-page mechanism, superseded by the generic `Layout` model (see Layout system integration bullet above and Puck Integration section). Dropped from `001_initial.sql` and from the shared test DB; its default block arrangements were carried forward as each type's `publishByDefault` starter so on-site appearance didn't change.

**Permissions**

`shop.access` (read-only GETs across orders/products/customers - every admin route below marked "or access" accepts this in place of its normal key), `shop.manage` (supersedes every other shop key - settings, email templates, tax/shipping config), `shop.products` (products/categories/tags/collections/CSV import-export CRUD), `shop.orders` (orders/refunds/manual payment confirmation), `shop.customers` (customer list/detail), `shop.discounts` (coupons/automatic discounts), `shop.reports` (tax/revenue reports, no read-only fallback). Enforced via `modules/shop/lib/access.ts`'s `requireShopUser(key, {allowAccess?})`/`hasShopPermission`. Page-layout editing is **not** one of these any more - since it moved onto the core Layout system, it's gated by core `layouts.manage` instead (same as Directory/Gazette/Boards' own layout types), not any `shop.*` key.

**API Routes** (all served through `/api/m/shop/…` via the generated router)

Public (`/api/m/shop/public/…`, unauthenticated unless noted; mutating ones rate-limited via a module-owned in-memory limiter in `lib/rate-limit.ts` - not table-backed like contact-form's, since a rate-limit-only IP column on shp_back_in_stock_subscriptions would be a schema change for a secondary guard; resets on cold start, doesn't share state across serverless instances):
- `GET /products` (filters: category/tag/collection/type/search/pagination, ACTIVE only), `GET /products/[slug]`, `GET /products/[slug]/related`, `GET /products/[slug]/upsells`, `GET /categories`, `GET /categories/[slug]`, `GET /collections`, `GET /collections/[slug]`, `GET /tags`.
- `GET /config` (client-safe config slice: currency, tax mode, enabled payment methods filtered by actual env presence, Stripe publishable key, checkout steps, shop status).
- `POST /cart/validate` (re-checks stock/price/status for client localStorage cart lines).
- `POST /checkout/session` (server-only totals - subtotal/discount/shipping/tax/total, never trusts client maths), `POST /checkout/apply-coupon`, `POST /checkout/payment-intent` (**PROTECTED** - creates the PENDING `shp_orders` row + item snapshot per Q8, then the provider's payment intent), `POST /checkout/confirm` (**PROTECTED** - confirms via the provider, idempotent PAID transition, triggers `fulfillPaidOrder`).
- `GET /orders/status?orderNumber=&email=` (guest lookup, both must match - no enumeration), `GET /downloads/[token]` (**PROTECTED** - token/expiry/download-limit checks, then streams the file bytes through this endpoint rather than redirecting, so the permanent underlying storage URL is never exposed to the client).
- `POST /back-in-stock` (idempotent subscribe), `DELETE /back-in-stock?token=` (**PROTECTED** - HMAC-signed unsubscribe token via `ENCRYPTION_KEY`, no DB lookup needed to validate it).

Member (`/api/m/shop/member/…`, `getMemberFromCookie()` gated): `GET /orders`, `GET /orders/[id]`, `GET/POST /addresses`, `PUT/DELETE /addresses/[id]`, `GET /gdpr-export` (internal-bearer only, `verifyInternalExportBearer` - called self-origin by core's member data-export assembler, feeds the `memberExtensions.dataExportPath` manifest entry).

Webhooks (`/api/m/shop/webhooks/…`, unauthenticated, signature-verified, **PROTECTED**): `POST /stripe` (verifies `STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET`, handles `payment_intent.succeeded`/`payment_intent.payment_failed`/`charge.refunded`), `POST /paypal` (verifies via PayPal's own verify-webhook-signature endpoint using `PAYPAL_WEBHOOK_ID`, handles `PAYMENT.CAPTURE.COMPLETED`/`PAYMENT.CAPTURE.REFUNDED`). Both idempotent - `markOrderPaid`'s `WHERE payment_status != 'PAID'` clause makes a replayed event a no-op.

Cron (`/api/m/shop/cron/…`, `CRON_SECRET` bearer): `GET/POST /low-stock-alerts` - daily 07:00, also covers Q11 import-job retention (30 days) and Q8 abandoned-PENDING-order pruning (24h).

Admin (`/api/m/shop/admin/…`, session + permission gated per route above): full CRUD for `products` (+ `[id]/related`, `[id]/upsells`, `export`/`import-template`/`import`(+`[id]` status poll)), `categories`, `tags`, `collections`, `tax-classes`, `tax-zone-rates`, `shipping-zones`(+ nested rates GET), `shipping-rates`, `coupons`, `automatic-discounts`; `orders` (list+manual-create, `[id]` detail, `[id]/status` (**PROTECTED** - decrements stock for pre-order items on SHIPPED per addendum B.4), `[id]/notes`, `[id]/email`, `[id]/refund` (**PROTECTED** - per-item, validates against refundedQty, calls the provider), `[id]/confirm-payment`); `customers` (list, `[id]` keyed by URL-encoded email - no dedicated table); `reports/tax`(+`?format=csv`)/`reports/revenue`; `dashboard-widget`; `email-templates`; `back-in-stock`; `settings` (shopConfig read/merge-update). Layout editing for all six page types goes through the core `/api/admin/layouts*` routes now (see Layout system integration bullet above) - there is no shop-specific layout-editing route any more (`admin/page-layouts/[key]` retired along with the table it served).

**Payment providers** (`modules/shop/lib/payments/`, **PROTECTED - entire directory**)
- `provider.ts` - the `ShpPaymentProvider` interface (`createIntent`/`confirmPayment`/`refundOrder`/optional `handleWebhook`) every provider implements.
- `stripe.ts` - `stripe` npm SDK (new core dependency, see below), no `apiVersion` pinned (uses the account's dashboard default rather than guessing a literal date string the installed major might reject), server always re-fetches the PaymentIntent and validates its own status **and** amount/currency against the order before trusting a client "confirmed" claim.
- `paypal.ts` - raw REST, no SDK (spec's own instruction, keeps the bundle lean), OAuth token cached in-memory with expiry, sandbox/live base URL switches on `PAYPAL_MODE`, capture amount/currency checked against the order on confirm.
- `bank-transfer.ts`/`cash.ts` - instructions-from-config intents, `confirmPayment` always fails (admin confirms manually via the order detail page's "Confirm payment" action), refunds are manual-only.
- `registry.ts` - `paymentProviders: Record<ShpPaymentMethod, ShpPaymentProvider>` lookup used by every route above.

**Sanctioned core diffs** (all outside `modules/shop/`, each minimal/isolated, flagged PROTECTED in-code):
- `package.json`/`package-lock.json` - added `stripe` (^22.x) as a core runtime dependency. Modules can't add their own npm dependencies (they compile inside core's Next build); precedent: `shiki` for Gazette, `leaflet`/`leaflet.markercluster` for Directory.
- `proxy.ts`'s `buildCsp()` - added `https://js.stripe.com` to `script-src`, `https://api.stripe.com` to `connect-src`, and a new `frame-src 'self' https://js.stripe.com https://hooks.stripe.com` directive (didn't exist before - Stripe Elements renders card fields and 3D Secure challenges in hidden iframes).
- Product image filing (`lib/media/product-media.ts`, `reorganiseProductMedia(productId)`): runs on every product `PUT` after the media/category writes. Files each `IMAGE` in `shp_product_media` into the core media library under **Shop / <master category> / <product-slug><n>** (`<n>` = 1-based position; no master → "Uncategorised"), via core's `getOrCreateFolderByPath(['Shop', <name>])` + `moveOrRenameMedia(id, {targetFolderId, newName, exactName:true, collision:'replace'})`. Only urls resolving to a managed core `Media` row are moved (external urls / video embeds left as-is); the row's `url` is rewritten to the relocated one. Idempotent (an already-filed image is a no-op) and best-effort per image (one relocate failure doesn't fail the save). The editor refetches after save so thumbnails follow the moved blobs. `exactName` keeps the stored key nanoid-free so the url reads `…/shop/<category>/<slug><n>.<ext>` exactly.
- `lib/media/upload.ts` - purely additive `NonImageUploadMode` type + `validateNonImageUpload(mimeType, sizeBytes, mode)` export for the digital-file upload path (declares its own mime/size allowlist, skips the sharp image-decode sniff entirely since there's no universal "valid PDF/zip" magic-byte check the way there is for images). The existing image-only `validateUpload`/`uploadMedia`/`deleteMedia`/`downloadMedia`/`saveMediaRecord` are untouched. Shop's digital files are **not** wired into the core `Media` table at all (no `saveMediaRecord` call) - they're stored in shop's own `shp_digital_files` table via `uploadMedia()`'s returned key/url only, since they're not part of core's page/logo Media referencing system.
- `.env.example` - added the seven Stripe/PayPal env var rows (all optional; a payment method with unset keys is filtered out of `enabledPaymentMethods` server-side, never offered at checkout - `modules/shop/lib/env.ts`'s `isStripeConfigured`/`isPayPalConfigured`).
- `app/api/admin/env/route.ts`'s `ALLOWED_KEYS` - added the same seven Stripe/PayPal vars so they're settable through the core env-var UI/API (Vercel project env vars, admin-only per `isAdmin()`). `lib/notifications/deployment.ts` gained a `PAYMENT_KEYS` set feeding `labelForEnvKeys()` → "Payment provider keys updated" on the existing deployment-needed notification.

**Admin pages** (`/cactus-admin/m/shop/…`)

`products` (list w/ search + back-in-stock subscriber-count column linking to the filtered `back-in-stock` view, Export/Import-template buttons, an "Import CSV" button opening `ImportModal.tsx` - upload → auto-detects header mismatches via `headerMatchesFormat()` and only then shows a column-mapping step → polls job progress, recent-imports log), `products/[id]` (editor - pricing/inventory/pre-order section/digital-file upload (`POST /admin/digital-files`, reuses core's `validateNonImageUpload`/`uploadMedia`)/image gallery via `MediaPickerModal.tsx` (browses + uploads to core's shared `/api/admin/media` library)/categories-tags-collections checkboxes + a **Master category** dropdown (options = the currently-ticked categories; unticking the master clears it; the `PUT` folds a stray master back into `categoryIds`)/SEO/**Recommendations panel** (`ProductPicker.tsx` search-to-add + reorder for related products, upsells, and the shared auto-exclude list, wired to the existing `[id]/related`/`[id]/upsells` routes)), `categories`, `collections` (both flat list + inline rename/delete, no drag-reorder UI yet), `orders` (status-tab filters incl. a `PRE_ORDER` tab), `orders/[id]` (items table, a "Refund items" button opening `RefundModal.tsx` (per-item quantity inputs pre-filled against remaining refundable qty, reason field, provider-aware copy for manual methods, one batched call to `POST .../refund`), financial summary, shipping address, "Confirm payment" for bank-transfer/cash, notes, email log, digital download tokens, and a Customer Communications section that renders only when another module - e.g. Reply Catcher - actually contributes to the `shop.order-messages` extension point), `customers`, `customers/[id]`, `discounts` (Coupons/Automatic tabs via the shared core `TabStrip`, real forms - not `prompt()` - covering type incl. fixed-amount/free-shipping, expiry window, usage/per-customer limits, minimum order value, free-shipping threshold, priority; edit + delete on both coupons and automatic discounts), `reports` (Revenue/Tax tabs via the shared core `TabStrip`), `back-in-stock` (no nav entry - reached from the products list), `tax-shipping` (`TaxShippingScreen.tsx` - tax classes CRUD (new tax class's `code` auto-slugs from `name`, read-only until unlocked via a pencil button), zones (name + postcode-prefix list, empty list = catch-all matched when no other zone's prefix matches, so one zone can cover a whole country without listing postcodes) picker+detail, per-zone tax rate per class, per-zone shipping rates (flat/weight-banded/free) picker+detail). `ShopSettingsTab` renders on core `/cactus-admin/config`, internal `TabStrip` sub-tabs (General/Checkout/Payments/Notifications/Email templates) covering the full `ShpConfig` shape: store identity+units/SEO/shop status, tax mode+checkout rules (guest checkout, min/max order value, phone requirement, per-step checkout-steps editor, back-in-stock account prompt, pre-order mixed-cart behaviour), payment methods w/ env-presence indicators, order/low-stock alert emails, and the email-templates editor.

**Public pages** (`/shop/…`, via `publicBasePath: "shop"`)

`/shop` (index, resolves the `shopIndex` layout via `resolveThemeLayout`, honours `shopStatus` CLOSED), `/shop/products/[slug]` (resolves `shopProduct`, 404s if none published; `productSlug`/`productId`/`inStock` injected into `ShopProductDetail`/`ShopRelatedProducts`/`ShopUpsellProducts`/`ShopBackInStockForm` block props via `lib/inject-product-context.ts` - mirrors core's `resolveTemplateData` context-injection pattern for MenuBlock etc, since these blocks have no per-instance slug of their own in the stored template), `/shop/categories/[slug]` (resolves `shopCategory`, falls back to the original hardcoded plain grid when none published), `/shop/collections/[slug]` (resolves `shopCollection`, same fallback pattern), `/shop/cart` (resolves the `shopCart` layout via `resolveThemeLayout` and renders it with `getModuleLayoutPuckRscConfig('shopCart')`; the `<h1>Your cart</h1>` stays in the page shell; falls back to the original hardcoded client-side cart UI + coupon field + `ShopUpsellProducts` when no `shopCart` layout is published, so never blank), `/shop/checkout` (resolves `shopCheckout`), `/shop/checkout/confirmation` (resolves `shopConfirmation`), `/shop/orders/[orderNumber]` (guest lookup form), `/shop/downloads/[token]` (friendly expired/limit-reached states, real download via the API route), `/shop/account/orders`(+`[id]`)/`/shop/account/addresses` (member-session-gated, 404 when Members disabled, redirect to `{memberAreaPath}/login?redirect=` when signed out).

**Extension Points**
- `core.admin-dashboard-widgets` (id `shop-summary`) - 30-day revenue/orders/AOV, low-stock chip, pending-manual-payment chip, active-pre-order chip.
- `members.account-section` (id `shop-orders`, **first module to use this point** - it existed in core unused until now) - "Orders & addresses" card linking to the member-area pages above.
- `core.menu-entity-provider` (id `shop`, `lib/menu-entity-provider.ts` exporting `shopMenuEntityProvider`) - lets the admin menu builder's "Module content" picker link to shop pages. Four kinds: Shop home (`/shop`), Product (`/shop/products/{slug}`, `publiclyVisible` only when status `ACTIVE`), Category (`/shop/categories/{slug}`), Collection (`/shop/collections/{slug}`). Same shape as Gazette/Directory/Boards providers; URL scheme mirrors `lib/sitemap.ts`.
- `shop.order-messages` (shop is the **consumer** here, not a publisher - no manifest entry needed) - the order detail page looks up any active module's `extensionPoints` for this point name and renders its contributed component with `orderId`/`orderNumber`/`customerEmail` props, mirroring the exact mechanism `members.admin-member-detail` already uses. Reply Catcher does not currently publish to this point (Q12 - shop builds only its own side; the reply-catcher-side contribution is out of scope), so the section never renders out of the box today.

**Puck Blocks** (all 18, registered in the generated `lib/puck/module-components.ts`)

`ShopProductGrid`, `ShopProductCard`, `ShopFeaturedCollection`, `ShopCategoryBrowser`, `ShopPromoBanner` (colour prop is a semantic token name, never hex), `ShopCartSummary` (client, reads localStorage cart, untagged - header-placement widget, not part of any `layoutTypes` page), `ShopCartFull` (client, full editable cart display - `CartFullClient` localStorage island wrapped by `components/puck/ShopCartFull.tsx`; ~33 look/behaviour options: rows/cards/table layout, spacing/dividers, optional heading, product-image toggle+size+radius, unit/line-price toggles, quantity control style (stepper/number/read-only), remove button text-or-bin, stock + pre-order badges, coupon field labels, item-count/subtotal toggles + labels, checkout button label/colour/text-colour via core `SiteColourField`/full-width/radius, empty-state copy + continue-shopping link, price-accent + panel colours; tagged `shopCart` (its layout type) but ALSO present on every core page via the all-module-blocks "Modules" category, so still droppable anywhere; ONE render path shared by editor and live for parity - editor render passes `preview` to seed sample lines with inert controls and no fetch, RSC render is a server wrapper passing only plain props into the client island, same trick as `ShopCartSummary`; no new API - reuses `/api/m/shop/public/cart/validate`, `/config`, `/checkout/apply-coupon`), `ShopCheckoutContact`/`ShopCheckoutShipping`/`ShopCheckoutPayment`/`ShopCheckoutReview` (all `[ANCHOR]` - `permissions:{delete:false,duplicate:false}` - client components sharing state via a sessionStorage-backed `checkout-state.ts` store since Puck blocks don't share React state; the Payment block owns the mounted Stripe Elements instance and listens for a `cactus-shop-place-order` window CustomEvent the Review block dispatches, since only Payment has access to `stripe.confirmPayment()`), `ShopOrderConfirmation`, `ShopProductDetail` (`[ANCHOR]`, add-to-cart non-removable; RSC render also emits the schema.org Product JSON-LD script tag), `ShopBackInStockForm` (auto-hidden via an `inStock` prop the product page injects), `ShopRelatedProducts`, `ShopUpsellProducts` (client, resolves upsells for every product currently in the cart client-side by calling the per-product upsells route once per cart line and merging/deduping), `ShopCategoryHeader`/`ShopCollectionHeader` (both `[ANCHOR]`, added with the layout system integration above - breadcrumb + name + description, re-fetched server-side from an injected `categorySlug`/`collectionSlug`).

**Configuration**

`ShpConfig` (`modules/shop/lib/config.ts`, Zod-validated, stored as the single `config` JSONB column on the `shp_settings` singleton, Q2): `currency`/`currencySymbol`/`storeEmail`/`orderNumberPrefix`/`weightUnit`/`dimensionUnit`, `taxMode` (INCLUSIVE\|EXCLUSIVE), `guestCheckoutEnabled`/`postPurchaseAccountPrompt`/`minimumOrderValue`/`maximumOrderValue`/`requirePhone`/`checkoutSteps` (ordered step array), `enabledPaymentMethods` (filtered by env presence at read time via `getAvailablePaymentMethods()`), `bankTransferInstructions`/`cashInstructions`, `adminOrderAlertEmail`/`lowStockAlertEnabled`/`lowStockAlertEmail`, `shopStatus` (OPEN\|BROWSE_ONLY\|CLOSED)/`shopClosedMessage`, `shopTitle`/`shopMetaDescription` (`shopBasePath` dropped per Q3 - fixed to `"shop"` via the manifest's `publicBasePath` instead of being runtime-configurable), `backInStockAccountPrompt`, `preOrderMixedCartBehaviour` (HOLD_ALL\|PROMPT_SPLIT).

**Admin dialogs**
The shop admin no longer calls the browser's `confirm()`/`prompt()`/`alert()`. `modules/shop/components/admin/dialogs.tsx` exports three promise-based hooks - `useConfirm()`, `usePrompt()`, `useAlert()` - each returning `[invoke, node]`: call `await invoke(...)` and render `{node}` once in the screen. Styling matches the module's other overlays (colour tokens only, `role="dialog"`/`aria-modal`, Escape cancels, Enter confirms, delete confirms use the `btn-danger` class). Wired through CategoriesScreen, CollectionsScreen, ProductsScreen (new-item name prompts), DiscountsScreen (delete confirms + save-error alerts), TaxShippingScreen (delete confirms), ProductEditor (upload/save-error alerts).

**Money formatting**
All prices render through one helper - `modules/shop/lib/money.ts` `formatMoney(amount, symbol='£')` - which coerces the string/number a price arrives as and always emits `symbol` + 2dp (e.g. `£7.99`). Storefront pages/blocks and order emails pass `config.currencySymbol`; admin screens (client-rendered, no server config) read it via `components/admin/use-currency-symbol.ts` `useCurrencySymbol()` (fetches `/api/m/shop/public/config` once, module-cached, `£` fallback). Prices are decimal pounds end to end (`NUMERIC(10,2)`); nothing is stored or displayed in pence (the Stripe `×100` in `lib/payments/stripe.ts` is API-only). Discount "value" cells format per type: `%` for PERCENTAGE, `formatMoney` for FIXED_AMOUNT, `—` for FREE_SHIPPING.

**External Integrations**
Stripe (Payment Intents + Elements + webhooks, `stripe` npm SDK), PayPal (Orders v2 REST API directly, no SDK), core Members system (optional, guest checkout always works regardless), core Media/upload pipeline (`uploadMedia()` reused for digital files, but not `saveMediaRecord` - see core diffs above), core email (`sendEmail` via `lib/email/index.ts`, shop owns its own `shp_email_templates` table rather than reusing core's `EmailTemplate`).

**Cron Jobs**
`0 7 * * *` → `/api/m/shop/cron/low-stock-alerts` - low-stock digest email (deduped via `low_stock_alerted_at`, re-arms on any stock_count write) + `shp_import_jobs` retention (30 days) + abandoned-PENDING-order pruning (24h, Q8). `CRON_SECRET` bearer-gated.

**Scripts**
None.

**Known Limitations** (v0.1.2 - flagged here rather than silently shipped as if finished)

- Categories/collections have no drag-to-reorder admin UI (the `position` column and API support it; only rename/delete are wired up in the screens).
- Reply Catcher's contribution to the `shop.order-messages` extension point is out of scope of this build (Q12) - the Communications tab section is real and will render the moment another module publishes to that point, but nothing does yet.
- The module-side rate limiter (`lib/rate-limit.ts`) is in-memory, not table-backed - resets on a cold start and doesn't share state across concurrent serverless instances. Acceptable for a secondary guard behind normal validation, but weaker than contact-form's DB-backed one.

v0.1.1 fixed five review findings from the original v0.1.0 build: Stripe/PayPal `confirmPayment` now validates charged amount/currency against the order (not just status/reference); `GET /downloads/[token]` streams the file through the endpoint instead of redirecting to the permanent storage URL; the `product`/`checkout` default page layouts now seed `ShopBackInStockForm`/`ShopUpsellProducts` (new installs only, per `ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING`); the product editor gained a real Recommendations panel, image picker, and digital-file upload; the Discounts screen, refund flow, CSV import, and page-layouts editor were all rebuilt from `prompt()`/raw-JSON placeholders into proper UI (see the Admin pages entry above for each).

### Twilio

Module `twilio` (repo `cactus-foundation-modules/twilio`), tablePrefix `tw_`, v0.1.6 (requiresCoreVersion 0.5.303 - needs the `admins.account-section` extension point). Twilio account integration: call forwarding for the account's incoming numbers, per-number call/message logs with recording playback, two-leg click-to-dial, and SMS delivery of login codes (via the core `smsProviders` hook, see Scripts above). No Puck blocks, no public pages, no cron.

- Env vars (manifest `requiredEnvVars`, all `required: false` so install isn't blocked before configuration): `TWILIO_ACCOUNT_SID`, `TWILIO_AUTH_TOKEN`. Managed through the module's core settings tab via `/api/admin/env` (module-declared keys are allowlisted generically). `TWILIO_PHONE_NUMBER` removed in v0.1.4 - the from-number is now picked from the account's numbers and stored in `tw_site_numbers` (default SMS number), not typed as an env var.
- Permission: `twilio.manage` (settings tab, nav entry, admin API routes).
- Manifest surfaces: `settingsTabs` → `TwilioSettingsTab` (credentials + connection status + phone-numbers picker: lists the account's incoming numbers with a Texts/No-texts capability badge, add/remove to site, radio choosing the default send-texts-from number - SMS-capable numbers only); `navEntries` → `/m/twilio` admin page; `smsProviders` → `lib/sms-provider.ts` `twilioSmsProvider` (`isConfigured` = credentials set AND an SMS-capable default site number selected, `sendSms` = `sendSiteSms`); `extensionPoints` → `members.account-section` `TwilioMemberSmsSection` (member SMS 2FA enrolment card) + `admins.account-section` `TwilioAdminSmsSection` (same card for the signed-in admin on the admin account page, no permission - self-service).
- Tables: `tw_forwarding_rules` (`phone_sid` unique, `phone_number`, `forward_to`, `enabled`, `greeting_message`, `greeting_voice`, `record_calls`, `show_called_number` - added by module migration `002_show_called_number.sql`), `tw_site_numbers` (account numbers added to the site: `phone_sid` unique, `phone_number`, `friendly_name`, `sms_capable`, `is_default_sms` with a partial unique index enforcing at most one default; metadata refreshed from Twilio on every listing, rows pruned when the number leaves the account, first/oldest SMS-capable number auto-promoted to default) and `tw_verification_codes` (enrolment codes: `subject_type` 'user'|'member' + `subject_id` unique pair, `phone_encrypted`, sha256 `code_hash`, 5 attempts, 10-min TTL). All three in `teardown`.
- API routes (all under `/api/m/twilio/`): `admin/status` (GET, connection test via account fetch; `fromNumber` = the default SMS site number or ''), `admin/numbers` (GET, Twilio incoming numbers merged with forwarding rules), `admin/site-numbers` (GET account numbers merged with site state + capability flags, also syncs stored metadata; POST `{ action: 'add'|'remove'|'set-default-sms', sid }` - add validates the sid against the live account listing and takes the capability flag from Twilio, never the client; set-default-sms rejects non-SMS-capable numbers), `admin/forwarding` (PUT, upserts rule and points the number's `VoiceUrl` at the voice webhook when enabled / clears it when disabled), `admin/greeting-preview` (POST, places an outbound call via `placeCall` from the row's Twilio number to a given number that `<Say>`s the unsaved greeting/voice - test-email-style preview), `admin/sms-2fa` (GET/POST send|verify/DELETE - self-service admin enrolment, writes `User.smsOtpPhoneEncrypted`; gated on `isSmsReady`, not just credentials), `member/sms-2fa` (same shape for members, upserts the `SMS` `MemberTwoFactor` row, same `isSmsReady` gate), `admin/calls` (GET `?number=`, recent calls to and from that number - two filtered `Calls.json` listings merged newest-first, completed recording SIDs attached from an account-wide `Recordings.json` listing keyed by call SID), `admin/messages` (GET `?number=`, same merge shape over `Messages.json`), `admin/recordings/[sid]` (GET, streams the recording MP3 through the site with the account's Basic auth so the browser never sees credentials; validates the `RE...` SID shape, `Cache-Control: private`), `admin/make-call` (POST `{ fromNumber, to, callMeAt }` - two-leg click-to-dial: validates both numbers E.164 and `fromNumber` against the live account listing (must be voice-capable), places a call to the admin from that number whose TwiML `<Gather>`s one digit then hits `webhooks/outbound-connect?to=`), `webhooks/outbound-connect` (POST, X-Twilio-Signature-validated over the full URL including the query string; on any digit returns `<Dial callerId="<From = the site's Twilio number>">` to the E.164 `to`, else `<Hangup/>`), `webhooks/voice` (POST, X-Twilio-Signature-validated, returns TwiML: optional `<Say voice="...">` greeting (XML-escaped `greeting_message`, voice from the curated `lib/voices.ts` list) then `<Dial>` to the enabled rule's target - with `record="record-from-answer-dual"` when `record_calls`, and `callerId="<called number>"` when `show_called_number` so the forwarded leg shows the site's Twilio number instead of the caller's - else `<Reject/>`).
- `lib/twilio.ts` is a dependency-free REST client (Basic auth, `AbortSignal.timeout(15s)`): `sendSms(to, body, from)` (explicit from-number), `listIncomingNumbers` (includes `smsCapable`/`voiceCapable` from Twilio's capability flags), `listCallsForNumber`/`listMessagesForNumber` (To+From listings merged newest-first, capped 50; calls carry completed recording SIDs), `fetchRecordingAudio` (recording MP3 fetch with account auth, 30s timeout), `setNumberVoiceUrl`, `fetchAccountName`, `placeCall` (outbound call with inline TwiML), `escapeXml`, `validateTwilioSignature` (HMAC-SHA1, timing-safe). `lib/numbers.ts` owns the site-number store: `getSiteNumbers`, `addSiteNumber`, `removeSiteNumber`, `setDefaultSmsNumber`, `syncSiteNumbers`, `getDefaultSmsNumber`, `isSmsReady`, `sendSiteSms` (throws when no text-enabled number is selected - texts are only ever sent from an SMS-capable number).
- Admin page `/m/twilio` (`TwilioAdminScreen`): one core `TabStrip` tab per account number (label `phoneNumber · friendlyName`, logs lazy-loaded per tab, Refresh button in the strip's trailing slot), each tab holding a "Make a call" card (number to call + "your phone" input remembered in localStorage `twilio-call-me-at`, hits `admin/make-call`), a call log table (when/direction/from/to/status/length + a Listen button per completed recording swapping to an inline `<audio controls autoPlay>` on the `admin/recordings/[sid]` proxy) and a message log table (when/direction/from/to/status/body). Forwarding configuration moved to the Settings Twilio tab in v0.1.6: `TwilioForwardingSection` (rendered by `TwilioSettingsTab` below the phone-numbers picker once connected) keeps the per-number rows - forward-to, on/off, greeting textarea (max 500 chars), voice `<select>` (optgroups from `lib/voices.ts` `TWILIO_VOICES` - Basic/Polly Standard/Neural/Generative; server validates via `isValidVoice`), record-calls checkbox (recordings playable from the Twilio page's call log), show-this-number-as-caller-ID checkbox (with a you-won't-see-who-rang note), "Call me to preview" (shown when a greeting is typed: number input + button hitting `admin/greeting-preview`). The admin's own SMS login-code card moved off this `twilio.manage`-gated page to the admin account page via `admins.account-section` (`TwilioAdminSmsSection`, wrapping the shared `SmsTwoFactorCard` also used by the member section) so every admin can enrol, not just Twilio managers.

### Gemini Watermark Remover

Module `gemini-watermark-remover` (tablePrefix `gwr_`, v0.1.7, requiresCoreVersion 0.5.346). Locates the Google Gemini watermark and **erases it by reverse alpha-blend at a pixel-verified candidate position**, saving the cleaned result into a dedicated root `gemini-processed` folder in the core media library under its original filename. No database tables (the `gwr_` prefix is reserved but unused), no Puck blocks, no public pages, no cron, no settings tab. Declares no permissions of its own - reuses the core `media.upload` permission.

- **Why the v0.1.6 rewrite (drops MI-GAN):** v0.1.3-0.1.5 erased the mark with client-side MI-GAN inpainting, but MI-GAN *hallucinates* the hole from its surroundings, so when the sparkle sits on a sharp geometric line (e.g. a desk edge) it smears the edge into a blur. Root cause of the earlier "reverse-blend leaves residual" belief was actually the library's **adaptive detector drifting off the mark** (picking an 80px box above the true 96px mark on a 2816x1536 image), so the reverse-blend was applied at the wrong place. Fix: skip the adaptive detector for placement entirely - reverse-blend at the exact catalog position (`detectWatermarkConfig`+`calculateWatermarkPosition`) with the matching embedded alpha map. Reverse-blend reconstructs the true underlying pixels (edges intact) and never smears; worst case on a non-catalog size is a faint leftover, not a destructive smear.
- **Why the v0.1.7 rewrite (pixel-verified placement):** the v0.1.6 blind catalog erase backfired when Gemini shipped a second geometry for the same size. 2752x1536 exports now carry the mark 192px from the corner (`alphaVariant '20260520'`, weaker blend curve) while the catalog still answers 64px - so v0.1.6 left the real mark AND burnt a black sparkle where it reverse-blended clean pixels (reverse-blend on unmarked pixels = over-subtraction = dark stamp). v0.1.7 never erases blind: it builds candidate boxes (library's own `meta.position` pick, catalog position, 192px new-margin variant), scores each by Pearson correlation between the alpha map and box luminance (real mark ≥ ~0.25, unmarked texture ≤ ~0.17, threshold 0.2), then picks the blend curve by trial erase on a copy (lowest leftover |correlation| wins; the wrong curve leaves 0.4+, the right one ~0). Two rejection gates fall back to the server pipeline instead of touching pixels: presence below threshold (`unlocated`), or best trial residual ≥ 0.3 / ≥ the presence score (erase would burn rather than clean, seen on scaled non-official-size exports).
- **Processing is all client-side** (kills the old >4MB lossy pre-upload re-encode and upload-cap failures). `components/admin/WatermarkRemoverScreen.tsx`: `createImageBitmap` at full res → `detectWatermark` (canvas) → if a box is found, `eraseWatermark` (reverse-blend, no ONNX) → encode under the 4MB cap (output only) → POST with `mode=save-cleaned`. Any browser-path failure falls through to `mode=server-fallback`.
- `lib/detect.ts` - `detectWatermark(canvas, rgba)` calls `removeWatermarkFromImage` for the `meta.applied` yes/no gate **and** takes its `meta.position`/`meta.config` as a candidate, alongside the catalog answer and the 192px new-margin variant. Candidates are deduped, bounds-checked, presence-scored against the pristine pixels, and the winner's blend curve is picked by trial erase (see v0.1.7 note above). Returns `{found:true, box, alphaKey}`, `{found:false, unlocated:false}` (genuinely clean), or `{found:false, unlocated:true}` (mark exists but no safe local erase → caller uses server fallback). `residualVisibility.visible` is unreliable both ways, so it is not used.
- `lib/erase.ts` - `eraseWatermark(rgba,imgW,box,alphaKey)`: pure reverse alpha-blend (`original = (watermarked - a*logo)/(1-a)`), constants copied verbatim from the library's `blendModes.js`. Fetches the embedded alpha map via a cached `WatermarkEngine` (no network, no ONNX). Only pixels the alpha map actually tinted are touched. Also exports the verification maths: `scoreSparklePresence(rgba,imgW,box,alphaKey)` (Pearson correlation between alpha-map magnitude and box luminance over signal pixels) and `pickAlphaMap(rgba,imgW,box,keys)` (trial erase per candidate map on a copied patch, returns the key with the lowest leftover |correlation| plus that residual).
- `lib/remove.ts` - server-fallback reverse-blend wrapper (library `/node` path, unchanged maths), returns `residualVisible` from `meta.detection.residualVisibility.visible`. `lib/pilio-gwr.d.ts` - ambient types for `/node` + `/browser` entry points (`getAlphaMap` widened to accept variant-key strings like `'96-20260520'`).
- API route `POST /api/m/gemini-watermark-remover/remove` (`app/api/remove/route.ts`) - session + `media.upload` gated, media provider required (503 otherwise), multipart `file` (PNG/JPEG/WebP) + `mode`. `save-cleaned`: skip removal, `validateUpload`→`uploadMedia`→`saveMediaRecord`, return `{ status:'erased', media }` 201. `server-fallback`: run reverse-blend; no watermark → `{ status:'clean', reason }` 200 (saves nothing); else save + `{ status: residualVisible ? 'partial' : 'removed', media }` 201. **Honesty gate: never returns a clean `removed` when residual is still visible.**
- Core deps: `@pilio/gemini-watermark-remover` (MIT), `sharp` `^0.34.5` (used by the server fallback). **`onnxruntime-web` was dropped from core `package.json`** (2026-07-14): MI-GAN was its only consumer, and the ONNX runtime the browser actually executes is vendored inside `@pilio/gemini-watermark-remover`'s own bundle. It was 132MB of `node_modules` - roughly half the 290MB Vercel build cache - contributing nothing to any bundle. The About-dialog credit for ONNX Runtime (`lib/about/credits.ts`) stays: the runtime still runs in the browser, just via the vendored copy. The `next.config.ts` `outputFileTracingIncludes[...] = ['./modules/*/assets/**']` glob now matches no module (kept: module-name-agnostic, future-proof).
- Admin page `/m/gemini-watermark-remover` (`app/cactus-admin/gemini-watermark-remover/page.tsx`, `media.upload` gated). `navEntries` → a plain ungrouped sidebar link. Outcome list statuses: erased / removed / partial / clean / error.
- Shipped as `cactus-foundation-modules/gemini-watermark-remover` (registered in `modules.json`; bump the tag pin at release), listed in the core README's Available modules, wiki page at `wiki/Gemini-Watermark-Remover.md`.
